<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Professor Minerva McGonagall</b>, <span class="template-c"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">O.M. (First Class)</a></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> was a <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scottish</a> <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>, the only daughter of <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Senior" title="Robert McGonagall Senior">Robert McGonagall</a> and witch <a href="/wiki/Isobel_Ross" title="Isobel Ross">Isobel Ross</a>. She also was the older sister of <a href="/wiki/Malcolm_McGonagall" title="Malcolm McGonagall">Malcolm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Junior" title="Robert McGonagall Junior">Robert Jnr</a>. Minerva attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> and was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>, but it took the Sorting Hat five and a half minutes to decide if she was Gryffindor or <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>, which made her a <a href="/wiki/Hatstall" title="Hatstall">Hatstall</a>. During her seventh year, she was appointed <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Girl</a>.   
</p><p>After her education, Minerva worked for two years at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and later returned to Hogwarts, where she became <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a>. Though she wasn't a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, Minerva greatly helped the Ministry of Magic's resistance through spying on <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and bringing the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> crucial information on their activities. 
</p><p>Eventually, Minerva became concurrently, at differing times, <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Headmaster" title="Deputy Headmaster">Deputy Headmistress</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Headmaster" title="Hogwarts Headmaster">Headmistress of Hogwarts</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, she opposed <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">High Inquisitor of Hogwarts</a>. She also protected the students from <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> from 1997 until 1998. As part of the Order of Phoenix's new resistance movement, Minerva fought in several battles of both wars, including the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, where she led the resistance against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>.
</p><p>Minerva survived the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> and continued her job as Headmistress, a title she still held as of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>'s time at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-CC41_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC41-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was born on <a href="/wiki/4_October" title="4 October">4 October</a> to <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Senior" title="Robert McGonagall Senior">Robert McGonagall</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Presbyterianism" title="Presbyterianism">Presbyterian</a> minister, and his wife <a href="/wiki/Isobel_Ross" title="Isobel Ross">Isobel Ross</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>. She was the couple's first child and was named after <a href="/wiki/Minerva" title="Minerva">her mother's grandmother</a>, a very powerful witch. By then, her parents lived on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Caithness" title="Caithness">Caithness</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scottish Highlands</a>, in a village where mostly Muggles lived.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Her birth proved both a joy and a crisis: Isobel had given up the use of her <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> for her love of Robert and never told him about her <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">nature</a> as she was afraid to mar the bliss of their wedding. However, the infant Minerva displayed small but noticeable signs of magic from her earliest hours. She had <a href="/wiki/Underage_magic" title="Underage magic">no control of her magic</a> and thus inadvertently <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">summoned</a> toys that had been left on upper shelves to her cot, made the <a href="/wiki/McGonagalls%27_cat" title="McGonagalls&#39; cat">family cat</a> do her bidding, and her<a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Snr%27s_bagpipes" title="Robert McGonagall Snr&#39;s bagpipes"> father's bagpipes</a> play themselves which would cause her to chuckle happily. Thus, Isobel often secluded herself with Minerva for days at a time. She knew she must confess to her husband about their daughter's <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizarding abilities</a> and so she finally did, explaining everything to Robert and telling him that they were bound by the <a href="/wiki/International_Statute_of_Wizarding_Secrecy" title="International Statute of Wizarding Secrecy">International Statute of Secrecy</a> and that they must conceal the truth about their magical abilities for their safety.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two parents remained together despite the shocking revelation, but their trust never was the same, much to the sadness of their perceptive daughter. She later had two brothers, <a href="/wiki/Malcolm_McGonagall" title="Malcolm McGonagall">Malcolm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Junior" title="Robert McGonagall Junior">Robert Jnr</a>, who revealed magical ability in due course. As a child, Minerva helped her mother conceal from her father the accidents and embarrassments the young witch's magic sometimes caused. She was very close to her Muggle father, whom in temperament she resembled more than her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On Minerva's eleventh birthday, Minerva received her <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_acceptance_letter" title="Hogwarts acceptance letter">admittance letter</a> from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, at the time <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">headed</a> by <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>. Before coming to the school, she visited <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> and purchased her wand from <a href="/wiki/Ollivanders" title="Ollivanders">Ollivander's</a> Wand Shop. The <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_wand" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s wand">wand</a> she selected was an unusual specimen, 9 and a half inches, <a href="/wiki/Fir" title="Fir">fir</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dragon_heartstring" title="Dragon heartstring">dragon heartstring</a>. Now free to be with her kind and to exercise her talents, Minerva saw how her mother sobbed that day, not only out of pride, but also out of envy.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years">Hogwarts years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>At the age of eleven, Minerva attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. During her <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting</a>, she proved to be a <a href="/wiki/Hatstall" title="Hatstall">hatstall</a>: the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> spent five-and-a-half minutes wavering between <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> before deciding to place her in the former. Minerva's school career overlapped by two years with that of <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>, and the two students enjoyed an excellent relationship, both then and in later years.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva was quickly recognised as the most outstanding student of her year with a particular talent for <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>. By the end of her education at Hogwarts, she had achieved an impressive record: top grades in <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a>, <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Girl</a>, and winner of the <i><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_Today_Most_Promising_Newcomer_award" title="Transfiguration Today Most Promising Newcomer award">Transfiguration Today Most Promising Newcomer award</a></i>. Under the guidance of her inspirational Transfiguration teacher, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, Minerva had managed to become an <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>; her animal form, with its distinctive markings (tabby cat, square spectacles markings around eyes) were duly logged in the Ministry of Magic's <a href="/wiki/Animagus_Registry" title="Animagus Registry">Animagus Registry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva played for <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> in her student years, in which she proved to be gifted. However, she suffered a nasty fall in her final year: a foul during the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor</a> versus <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin</a> match which would decide the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a> winner. This event left her with a concussion, several broken ribs, and a lifelong desire to see Slytherin crushed on the Quidditch pitch.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_heartbreak">Early heartbreak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early heartbreak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Early heartbreak"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/YoungMcGonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172122" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="154" height="235" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="YoungMcGonagall.jpg" data-image-key="YoungMcGonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/YoungMcGonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20150810172122" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/YoungMcGonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172122" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/YoungMcGonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20150810172122" decoding="async" width="154" height="235" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="YoungMcGonagall.jpg" data-image-key="YoungMcGonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/YoungMcGonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20150810172122" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:YoungMcGonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A younger Minerva McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After graduating from Hogwarts, Minerva was offered a position at the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> of the British <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. She returned to her <a href="/wiki/McGonagall_manse" title="McGonagall manse">family's manse</a> to spend one last summer with her family before moving to <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. During these months an eighteen-years old Minerva met <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">Dougal McGregor</a>, a local <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, who was the handsome, clever, and funny son of a <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor%27s_father" title="Dougal McGregor&#39;s father">local farmer</a>. The two shared a sense of humour, argued fiercely, and suspected mysterious depths in each other. Minerva fell head-over-heels in <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> with McGregor, being the first and only time in her life that she might have been said to lose her head. Eventually, McGregor proposed to Minerva on a ploughed field and she accepted his offer.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>That night, however, Minerva was unable to tell her parents of her engagement. Thinking about her future, she realised that wedding a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> who didn't know that she was a witch would mean Minerva would follow her mother's footsteps and live unhappily with her wand locked away, shredding all of her ambitions. Early next morning, Minerva went to tell McGregor she had changed her mind and could not <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">marry</a> him, aware that if she broke the International Statute of Secrecy and told him why, she would lose the job at the Ministry for which she was giving him up. She could give him no good reason for her change of heart, leaving McGregor devastated and left for <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> three days later. These months were to prove some of the most difficult of Minerva’s life.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Employment">Employment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Employment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Employment"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Though her feelings for the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> were affected by the fact that she had recently suffered an emotional crisis, Minerva didn't much enjoy her home in London and workplace, where some of her co-workers had an ingrained anti-Muggle bias. Given her adoration of her Muggle father and continuing love for Dougal, she deplored these ideas. Despite this, Minerva was among the most efficient, gifted employees in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> and became fond of her much older boss, <a href="/wiki/Elphinstone_Urquart" title="Elphinstone Urquart">Elphinstone Urquart</a>. After two years at the Ministry, she was offered a prestigious promotion, yet found herself turning it down as she missed her home in <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 274px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/YoungMinerva.png/revision/latest?cb=20190401175135" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="272" height="132" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="YoungMinerva.png" data-image-key="YoungMinerva.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/YoungMinerva.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20190401175135" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/YoungMinerva.png/revision/latest?cb=20190401175135" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/YoungMinerva.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20190401175135" decoding="async" width="272" height="132" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="YoungMinerva.png" data-image-key="YoungMinerva.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/YoungMinerva.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20190401175135" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:YoungMinerva.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva in her earlier years as a <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Instead, Minerva sent an owl to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, asking whether she might be considered for a teaching post. The owl returned within hours, offering her a job in the Transfiguration department, under Head of Department, Albus Dumbledore. Through her efforts and work, Minerva proved to be a inspirational yet strict teacher, maintaining control of her students with a stern hand that made her someone not to be crossed.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By this time, Minerva was shocked to learn from her oblivious mother (in the middle of a chatty letter of local news) that Dougal had married the daughter of another farmer. Albus discovered his former student and colleague in tears in her classroom late that evening, and she confessed the whole story to him. He offered both comfort and told Minerva some of his own family history, previously unknown to her. The confidences exchanged that night between were to form the basis of a lasting friendship.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Among her first students were <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a>, the latter of whom was frequently in trouble with Minerva for retaliating to vicious gossip about her <a href="/wiki/Corvus_Lestrange_(V)" title="Corvus Lestrange (V)">half-brother</a>'s death. A notable example of this is when Leta hexed a fellow student with the dark charm <i><a href="/wiki/Oscausi" title="Oscausi">Oscausi</a></i> during her third year, after the other girl had been speaking ill of Leta behind her back. Minerva was called upon to fix the situation, but Leta ran from her and Minerva was forced to chase her around the school, all the while docking points (Minerva ended up docking a total of 200 points). When she couldn't find Leta, Minerva removed the spell from the girl but promptly restored it with an irritated "Whisht!" when the girl continued to badmouth Leta.<sup id="cite_ref-COGS_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COGS-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During Gellert Grindelwald's rise, Minerva still taught at Hogwarts and was a close confidant to Dumbledore. She was quite critical of the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>'s involvement at Hogwarts and was furious when <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a> and a team of <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> interrupted Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> lesson, protesting that this was "a school." However, her protests fell on deaf ears and she was forced to escort the students from the <a href="/wiki/Classroom_3C" title="Classroom 3C">classroom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Through her early years at Hogwarts, Minerva remained close friends with her former boss in the Ministry, Elphinstone. During one visit, he proposed marriage to Minerva at <a href="/wiki/Madam_Puddifoot%27s_Tea_Shop" title="Madam Puddifoot&#39;s Tea Shop">Madam Puddifoot's Tea Shop</a>. Surprised, embarrassed, and still in love with Dougal, she declined. However, the two still remained in contact for years.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on in her career, Minerva rose to the position of <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Transfiguration" title="Head of Transfiguration">Head</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_department" title="Transfiguration department">Transfiguration department</a>. Her lessons consisted of but were not limited to <a href="/wiki/Match_to_needle_spell" title="Match to needle spell">match to needle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vera_Verto" title="Vera Verto">animal to water goblet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Beetle_Buttons" title="Beetle Buttons">beetle to button</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mice_to_Snuffboxes" title="Mice to Snuffboxes">mouse to snuffbox</a> transformations, as well as <a href="/wiki/Switching_Spell" title="Switching Spell">Switching Spells</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Spell" title="Vanishing Spell">Vanishing</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">Conjuring</a>. Furthermore, Minerva was appointed the position of <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a>, the house in which she used to reside whilst studying at Hogwarts. After he became Headmaster, Dumbledore would later on in his career also trust her enough to allow her to become <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Headmaster" title="Deputy Headmaster">Deputy Headmistress</a> of the school and fill in for him on the occasions of his absence.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="First_Wizarding_War_(1970-1981)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281970-1981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1970-1981)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>Oh yes, everyone’s celebrating, all right. You’d think they’d be a bit more careful, but no – even the Muggles have noticed something’s going on. It was on their news. I heard it. Flocks of <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owls</a> ... shooting stars ... Well, they’re not completely stupid. They were bound to notice something. Shooting stars down in <a href="/wiki/Kent" title="Kent">Kent</a> – I’ll bet that was <a href="/wiki/Dedalus_Diggle" title="Dedalus Diggle">Dedalus Diggle</a>. He never had much sense.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>You can’t blame them, We’ve had precious little to celebrate for eleven years.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>I know that, but that’s no reason to lose our heads. People are being downright careless, out on the streets in broad daylight, not even dressed in Muggle clothes, swapping rumours.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; McGonagall's reaction to the wizarding world's celebration of Voldemort's downfall<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>After the first rise of <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Minerva took part in fighting back against Lord <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, though she still taught at Hogwarts during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Previously, she was suspicious of Riddle in spite of the fact that she wasn't his teacher and thus shared her fears with Dumbledore in private. Even so, McGonagall chose to not join the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, which was seen as a renegade outfit by the Ministry at the time. Instead, unbeknownst to her students, she spent many nights spying for them in the guise of a tabby cat, bringing the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> crucial information on the activities of Voldemort's followers.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/de/Lily_Sorted.png/revision/latest?cb=20130819021410" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily Sorted.png" data-image-key="Lily_Sorted.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/de/Lily_Sorted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130819021410" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/de/Lily_Sorted.png/revision/latest?cb=20130819021410" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/de/Lily_Sorted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130819021410" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily Sorted.png" data-image-key="Lily_Sorted.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/de/Lily_Sorted.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130819021410" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_Sorted.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva placing the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> on Lily Evans</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite her involvement in the Ministry's efforts to contain the threat of the Dark Lord's rise to power, Minerva got through the war unscathed. However, she suffered personal bereavements: the loss of her brother <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Junior" title="Robert McGonagall Junior">Robert</a>; of two of her favourite students, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>; and of <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">Dougal McGregor</a>, who was murdered in a random anti-Muggle attack by the Death Eaters, along with <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor%27s_wife" title="Dougal McGregor&#39;s wife">his wife</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor%27s_children" title="Dougal McGregor&#39;s children">children</a>. This last news was a terrible blow to Minerva, who wondered if she would have been able to save him if she had married him.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Concurrently, as the war raged outside the castle walls, the school was plagued by a series of <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a> inadvertently unleashed by one of the students, <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, who began to meddle with the five fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>. Like the rest of the faculty, Professor McGonagall did everything she could to protect the students, although they were ultimately unable to prevent the injury of several students and the death of a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> student named <a href="/wiki/Duncan_Ashe" title="Duncan Ashe">Duncan Ashe</a>; this all led to Jacob's <a href="/wiki/Discipline_at_Hogwarts#Expulsion" title="Discipline at Hogwarts">expulsion</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Protection_of_Harry_Potter">Protection of Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Protection of Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Protection of Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>These people will never understand him! He'll be famous -- a legend -- I wouldn't be surprised if today was known as Harry Potter day in the future -- there will be books written about Harry -- every child in our world will know his name!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva discussing Harry Potter's future with his Muggle relatives<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161127213858" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="153" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-image-key="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161127213858" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161127213858" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161127213858" decoding="async" width="235" height="153" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-image-key="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161127213858" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva and Dumbledore delivering Harry to the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>' home</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, baby <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> <i>"defeated"</i> Lord Voldemort in his family home at <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> after his parents James and Lily Potter (both members of the Order of the Phoenix) were murdered whilst protecting their son from harm. The defeat of Voldemort ultimately ended the war and his followers were arrested and those that escaped went into hiding.
</p><p>Minerva travelled to <a href="/wiki/Surrey" title="Surrey">Surrey</a> and there spent an entire day observing the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursley family</a> seeing whether or not they met the standards of looking after Harry as they were his only living relatives with his parents now dead. What she saw horrified her; the Dursleys couldn't have been any less like Lily and James if they had tried. She was thus present, along with <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> placed Harry on the Dursleys' doorstep, despite her objections to leaving him with these <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>, whom she considered to be the "worst kind" of them. She kept a close eye on Harry from time to time during his early childhood, as did the members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Between_the_wars_(1981-1995)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Between_the_wars_.281981-1995.29">Between the wars <span class="template-c">(1981-1995)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1995)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981-1995)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Transfiguration_class1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141018192503" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Transfiguration class1.gif" data-image-key="Transfiguration_class1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Transfiguration_class1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141018192503" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Transfiguration_class1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141018192503" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Transfiguration_class1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141018192503" decoding="async" width="241" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Transfiguration class1.gif" data-image-key="Transfiguration_class1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bd/Transfiguration_class1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141018192503" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Transfiguration_class1.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall teaching a second year Transfiguration class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> had ended, Minerva continued on with her career at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, carrying on teaching the art of Transfiguration. Elphinstone, who had never ceased to love her, proposed every now and then until she finally accepted after Dougal's death. Their engagement happened during a summertime stroll around the lake in the Hogwarts grounds. The retired Elphinstone bought a small cottage for the two of them in Hogsmeade, whence Minerva could travel easily to work every day. Although the couple had no children, her nieces and nephews visited often. This was a period of great fulfilment for Minerva.
</p><p>In 1985, three years into their marriage, Elphinstone died from a <a href="/wiki/Venomous_Tentacula" title="Venomous Tentacula">Venomous Tentacula</a> bite.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Minerva, who couldn't bear to remain alone in their cottage, packed her things after her husband's funeral and returned to her first-floor study in Hogwarts Castle. It is unknown whether she still owns the cottage. Always a brave and private person, Minerva poured all her energies into her work and few people – excepting perhaps Albus – ever realised how much she suffered.
</p><p>During the second year of the <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">sibling</a> of <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a> when missing, the individual asked Minerva about it as she was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_House" title="Head of House">Head of the Gryffindor House</a>. She first asked if Jacob's sibling had seen him in the Hogwarts Express and if he had been acting strange and after learning that they didn't but <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a> did and Ben seemed fine even though he was always a bit odd. She mentioned that the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> may have changed Ben and slightly chastised Jacob's sibling for their attempt to enter the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vault</a>, asking them if they had learnt anything that said of a threat beyond the door and appealed to them that this involved all of Hogwarts, not just Jacob. Learning that they had found and read a message about an <a href="/wiki/Ice_Knight" title="Ice Knight">Ice Knight</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vanished_Stairs" title="Vanished Stairs">Vanished Stairs</a>, Minerva said she will discuss this with Dumbledore and accidentally revealed that she and the other teachers had once dealt with the Cursed Ice, which she quickly covered by telling Jacob's sibling that he is free to help in the search of Ben and ask for him to tell her personally should he succeed, promising to reward him.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime later, Minerva asked for Jacob sibling's help to find Gryffindor Broom Wax which had been misplaced by the keeper should they be a Gryffindor. Accompanying Jacob's sibling to the Common Room, she congratulated them for their success and gave them twenty House Points for their effort. Later, impressed by their transfiguration talents, McGonagall offered to give them advanced transfiguration classes.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>If they were of another house and tried to infiltrate the Gryffindor Common Room, Minerva would catch them with Angelica but as they searched for Ben, she allowed them to get away unpunished. McGonagall and Snape eventually found the missing Ben Copper encased in Cursed ice and Jacob's Sibling and Rowan realised she knew more about the Cursed Ice than she revealed. Minerva was perplexed that the <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a> had no effect on the ice, noting on how they once could use it to shatter the ice, and even more so when Snape callously suggested they use <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Incendio</a> to melt the ice while also burning him to death, as she realises from how the Cursed Ice had began to expand throughout the school that someone had been tampering with the Vaults. Ignoring Snape's frustrated questioning of Dumbledore's whereabouts, Minerva and Snape used the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a> to successfully free Ben from the Cursed Ice, taking care to target as further as possible from his body.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Knowing Minerva was the only one left in the school with Dumbledore gone that could possibly teach them the <a href="/wiki/Revelio_Charm" title="Revelio Charm">Revelio Charm</a>, Jacob's Sibling turned to her to learn the spell. At first Minerva was baffled due to how advanced the charm was but ultimately agreed to teach them if they proved themselves sufficiently adept, impressed by their desire to help Hogwarts and study Transfiguration. Finding their abilities to have reached the level required in the class, Minerva called them to have their private lesson and after Jacob's sibling successfully learned Revelio, Minerva congratulated them and noted the usefulness of the spell.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After learning that Bill Weasley had taught Jacob's sibling <i>Incendio</i>, Minerva was furious and scolded him heavily.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Protecting_the_Philosopher's_Stone"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Protecting_the_Philosopher.27s_Stone">Protecting the Philosopher's Stone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Protecting the Philosopher&#039;s Stone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Protecting the Philosopher&#039;s Stone"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Welcome to Hogwarts. The start-of-term banquet will begin shortly, but before you take your seats in the Great Hall, you will be Sorted into your houses.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva McGonagall introducing the first-year students of <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> to Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/McGonagall_students.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160304181637" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="McGonagall students.jpg" data-image-key="McGonagall_students.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/McGonagall_students.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160304181637" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/McGonagall_students.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160304181637" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/McGonagall_students.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160304181637" decoding="async" width="245" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="McGonagall students.jpg" data-image-key="McGonagall_students.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/McGonagall_students.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160304181637" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:McGonagall_students.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall welcomes first year students to Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In 1991 friend of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>, had the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> that was keeping him alive moved from his safe in <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> for safe keeping. Minerva contributed to the defences set up around the magical artefact by transfiguring an enormous <a href="/wiki/Chessboard_Chamber" title="Chessboard Chamber">chess set</a> and <a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">animating</a> it to behave as a normal Wizard's chess set would. As part of its protection duty, it required that the person or persons seeking to get past would have to take the place of a piece on the board and play an actual game of wizard's chess, at great physical risk to themselves. This larger than life version of <a href="/wiki/Wizard%27s_Chess" title="Wizard&#39;s Chess">Wizard's chess</a> is known to be brutally violent and sacrificial for wizards to have to take part in themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706040031" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-minerva sorting.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706040031" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706040031" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706040031" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-minerva sorting.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706040031" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-minerva_sorting.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva directing students during the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Also in this year, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, whom Minerva had been watching over for many years, would start his first year of education at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, not knowing this, as he did not know that he was a wizard. Once Harry eventually arrived at Hogwarts, after the delivery of many acceptance letters, Harry was Sorted into the house of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> which Minerva was head of. Harry was therefore again placed under the watchful eye and care of McGonagall.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though Minerva often maintained her strict persona in regards to the boy, she wasn't above bending the rules for him on occasion, such as when she caught him flying on a broomstick without proper supervision. Instead of expelling him, which was Madam Hooch's stated punishment for anyone caught doing so, Minerva instead took him to see <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Wood" title="Oliver Wood">Oliver Wood</a>, captain of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>, to comment on his prodigious skill with the broom. Harry made the team, remarkable for a first year, and became the youngest <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> in a century. She made arrangements for Harry to have a <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2000" title="Nimbus 2000">Nimbus 2000</a>, the fastest broomstick of the time, for use during games and practices. However, several incidents marred the year.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706035111" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-mcgonagall classroom.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706035111" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706035111" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706035111" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-mcgonagall classroom.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706035111" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-mcgonagall_classroom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall chastising Harry and Ron for being late to class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At Hallowe'en, the festive feast was interrupted by the arrival of Professor Quirrell, who came charging in screaming about a troll loose in the dungeons before fainting dead away. After restoring calm, Dumbledore ordered all students to return to their dormitories while he and the teachers made their way to the dungeons. The troll was not there upon their entry, but a terrible racket from an upper floor provided a clue. Upon reaching the site, Minerva was shocked to discover a wrecked bathroom, an unconscious troll and three bedraggled first years, one of whom was her best student Hermione Granger. To her further shock, Hermione claimed that she had gone looking for the troll thinking she could handle it but would most assuredly have been killed had Harry and Ron not found her. Torn between anger and pride, Minerva took five points from Hermione but awarded five each to Harry and Ron for, as she put it, "sheer dumb luck." Over the Christmas period, she attended the Christmas feast and received a kiss on the cheek from a very drunk Hagrid; rather than admonish him, she instead giggled while blushing red in the face.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Transfiguration_homework.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170524232616" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Transfiguration homework.jpg" data-image-key="Transfiguration_homework.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Transfiguration_homework.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232616" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Transfiguration_homework.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170524232616" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Transfiguration_homework.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232616" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Transfiguration homework.jpg" data-image-key="Transfiguration_homework.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Transfiguration_homework.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232616" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Transfiguration_homework.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall being informed of the trio's suspicions someone was going to steal the Stone</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, her serious side appeared one night when she caught Draco Malfoy roaming the school at night. Dragging him by the ear, she sentenced him to detention and deducted twenty points from Slytherin when he claimed that Harry was also out of bed with an illegal baby dragon. Though the dragon in question was successfully released, Harry, Hermione and Neville were all caught and brought before McGonagall by Filch. Mad and disappointed with them, she told them all off before punishing them severely; a loss of fifty points each, 150 in total, and detention with Malfoy. This caused Gryffindor to drop to last in the House Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Towards the end of the year, McGonagall and the other teachers' protective enchantments down in the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone_chambers" class="mw-redirect" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone chambers">Philosopher's Stone chambers</a> would come to test when <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirrell</a> attempted to steal the Philosopher's Stone. Also testing and facing the enchantments were <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>. The trio was successful in stopping the stone being stolen and at the end of the school year, Gryffindor had won the house cup after receiving the most house points that year after getting bonus points for the trio's and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>'s bravery. Thus, for the first time in years, McGonagall's house was the current house cup champions. Her reaction wasn't documented, but it's assumed that she was pleased with their efforts as Professor Snape shook her hand with a very forced look of congratulations.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_second_opening_of_the_Chamber_of_Secrets">The second opening of the Chamber of Secrets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The second opening of the Chamber of Secrets">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: The second opening of the Chamber of Secrets"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>What does this </i>mean<i>, Albus?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>It means that the Chamber of Secrets is indeed open again.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The opening of the Chamber is confirmed after finding Colin Creevey petrified<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>In the beginning of the 1992 school term, Minerva had to deal with Harry and Ron, who crashed Mr Weasley's <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">Flying Ford Anglia</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>, due to the barrier to <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">Platform Nine and Three-Quarters</a> being sealed by <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> so the two couldn't board the train. This nearly exposed the wizarding world to Muggles, but Minerva was fairer than Snape, the one who brought the matter up in the first place. Minerva ultimately let them off with a mere detention and letters to their families. Also she didn't take any house points as Harry pointed out that term had not started yet when they took the car, which she confirmed and almost smiled at this remark.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161129042803" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161129042803" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall and other members of staff discover the declaration</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Minerva was present for the re-opening of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>. She, along with the rest of the teaching staff, scoured the castle for the Chamber, but to no avail. Minerva was worried over the messages left on the walls and was at a loss about what should be done. She also had to deal with the less than helpful <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, who had been hired for the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor. McGonagall had little liking or use for the man and by the end of the year was only one of the many staff members who utterly despised him. For example when he decorated the Great Hall in nauseatingly lurid pink hearts for Valentine's Day, she was observed to have a muscle twitching noticeably in her face. Throughout the year, two of Minerva's students, Hermione Granger and Colin Creevey were Petrified along with the House ghost Nearly Headless Nick.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the final weeks of that school year, Minerva served as temporary <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmistress</a> of Hogwarts after the Board of Governors, under Lucius Malfoy's influence, suspended Dumbledore for failing to stop the attacks against the students. She was also quite shaken and softened up, as when Harry and Ron tried to sneak off to investigate the matter but were caught by herself. She let them off under the belief that they were trying to visit a <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> Hermione, though she normally would punish them with detention.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170629204309" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170629204309" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170629204309" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170629204309" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170629204309" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-15204.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The professors moments after Ginny Weasley was kidnapped by the monster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>All students to return to their House dormitories at once. All teachers return to the staff room. Immediately, please.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva's emergency announcement<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> was later taken into the Chamber of Secrets, where "<i>her skeleton will lie in the chamber forever</i>", Minerva despairingly believed that they were facing the end of Hogwarts. Her temperament was not improved by the arrival of the hated Gilderoy Lockhart, who was completely oblivious to the worry of his fellow staff members, and immediately joined Professors Snape, Flitwick and Sprout in forcing him into a corner by recalling all of his boasts that he could deal with the monster easily. With him dealt with, as they couldn't care less if he succeeded or failed, the staff turned their attention to the thing they never thought would happen; the permanent closure of Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706043156" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-minera leaving feast.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706043156" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706043156" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706043156" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-minera leaving feast.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706043156" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-minera_leaving_feast.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall at the End-of-Term Feast celebrating the end of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thankfully, this terrible reality never came to pass. While McGonagall received Ginny's distraught parents in her office, along with a returned Albus Dumbledore, she was astonished to see Ginny herself walk in, accompanied by a slime-covered Harry, Ron and Lockhart, the ragged old Sorting Hat, Dumbledore's pet phoenix and the silver Sword of Godric Gryffindor. Harry then explained that he and Ron had gone into the Chamber to find Ginny, having realised the mystery, and had slain the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">monster</a> within. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> then declared the crisis over and sent Minerva down to the kitchens to organise a celebratory feast, which she subsequently attended with great joy as the monster was dead and Lockhart banished.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Escape_of_Sirius_Black">Escape of Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Escape of Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Escape of Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>Sir Cadogan, did you just let a man enter Gryffindor Tower?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Sir Cadogan</b>: "<i> Certainly, good lady!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>You — you did? But — but the password!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Sir Cadogan</b>: "<i>He had ‘em! Had the whole week’s, my lady! Read ‘em off a little piece of paper!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>Which person, which abysmally foolish person wrote down this week’s passwords and left them lying around?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Minerva's shock at Sirius Black entering the castle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>The summer of 1993 also saw the <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes" title="Azkaban escapes">escape</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. When the school year began in September, Minerva had to deal with the effects that the Dementors had on her students, such as Harry Potter. She also authorised <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> to use a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> in order to take extra classes, a decision that would prove more useful in future events that year. This year at Hogwarts would prove to be another difficult year with Dementors guarding the castle, though they were forbidden from entering the grounds properly by Dumbledore. Minerva heartily approved of this, as she despised the foul creatures.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the start of the year, when McGonagall demonstrated her <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form to her first class, she notes how quiet they were, as every class she demonstrated it to prior clapped. When Hermione explained about their first <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, McGonagall understood and asked her class which of them would be dying this year. Harry Potter raised his hand. McGonagall assured him that <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>'s predictions were a way of greeting her class and that no deaths of any students have occurred yet. To further put him at ease, she demonstrated one of her rare glimmerings of humour by stating that she still expected him to do his homework, but if he did die then she would excuse his not handing it in.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729002112" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gryffindor common room 1993.jpg" data-image-key="Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729002112" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gryffindor common room 1993.jpg" data-image-key="Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professor McGonagall and the residents of Gryffindor Tower in the common room after Sirius Black's break-in</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Throughout the year, Minerva assisted in guarding the school, yet nonetheless Black was able to infiltrate the castle. After Black had attacked the <a href="/wiki/Fat_Lady" title="Fat Lady">Fat Lady</a>, McGonagall tried to tell Harry that Black was after him, but was cut off by Harry, who told her that Mr Weasley had told him, before she could explain. Later in the year, Minerva was summoned to <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Tower" title="Gryffindor Tower">Gryffindor Tower</a> when Ron Weasley claimed to have been attacked by Black. She initially dismissed him as Black could not have possibly got in without the password (unaware that Hermione's cat, <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a>, befriended by Sirius and gave him a discarded list of passwords) but was rendered speechless when the new guardian, Sir <a href="/wiki/Cadogan" title="Cadogan">Cadogan</a>, confirmed that he had indeed let him in because he had the passwords written down. When <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> admitted to having written the passwords down, McGonagall banned him from future Hogsmeade visits for the rest of the year, gave him a detention, forbade anyone to give him the password into Gryffindor Tower and wrote to his grandmother. As a result, Neville received a <a href="/wiki/Howler" title="Howler">Howler</a> from her during breakfast.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
