<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170904130141" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Christmas Firebolt minerva.jpg" data-image-key="Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170904130141" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170904130141" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170904130141" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Christmas Firebolt minerva.jpg" data-image-key="Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170904130141" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Christmas_Firebolt_minerva.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry receives a Firebolt for Christmas that is soon confiscated by McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry received a <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Firebolt" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Firebolt">Firebolt</a> following the destruction of his Nimbus 2000, McGonagall had it confiscated to be "examined" because she believed it to have been sent by Black (and correctly so), and therefore lethally cursed (which was incorrect). This incident caused Harry and Hermione to have a row, because Hermione had alerted Minerva about the Firebolt. It was returned to him later after having been declared safe. During the Quidditch match against Ravenclaw, Draco Malfoy, Gregory Goyle, Vincent Crabbe, and Marcus Flint posed as <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> to sabotage Harry's performance, only to get struck down when Harry reflexively cast a Patronus Charm at them. Utterly furious at this downright trickery, she deducted fifty points from Slytherin and put the quartet in detention.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161127221739" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter Pottermore Harry Holding Quidditch Cup In A Crowd Moment.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127221739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161127221739" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127221739" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter Pottermore Harry Holding Quidditch Cup In A Crowd Moment.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127221739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_Pottermore_Harry_Holding_Quidditch_Cup_In_A_Crowd_Moment.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Gryffindor wins the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a> in 1994</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the spring of 1994, though disgusted by the Slytherin Quidditch team's dirty tactics during the final Quidditch match after witnessing <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> grab onto the end of Harry's Firebolt to stop him from catching the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Golden Snitch</a> (which infuriated her to the point where she stopped telling Lee Jordan off and actually joined him in firing furious comments at Malfoy), she witnessed the Gryffindor Quidditch team win the Quidditch Cup for the first time since <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie Weasley</a> had played for the team during his Hogwarts education. McGonagall was delighted by Gryffindor's victory, openly sobbing &#8212; even louder than the already sobbing Oliver Wood — into a Gryffindor Flag, but was upset to see <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Wood" title="Oliver Wood">Oliver Wood</a> leaving. Later on in the year, three students from her house &#8212; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> &#8212; would run into trouble when <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> returned to Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Triwizard_Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Triwizard Tournament">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Triwizard Tournament"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>The Yule Ball is of course a chance for us all to — er — let our hair down. But that does NOT mean that we will be relaxing the standards of behaviour we expect from Hogwarts students. I will be most seriously displeased if a Gryffindor student embarrasses the school in any way.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall introducing the Yule Ball<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>In the autumn of 1994, Hogwarts hosted the magical schools, the <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was selected as a Triwizard Champion, despite being under age and McGonagall worried for his safety after having looked after him for so many years. Minerva pleaded with Dumbledore and Crouch to withdraw Harry from the tournament, as the tournament was highly dangerous. But withdrawing would go against the rules of the tournament and Potter had to continue on, as there was a <a href="/wiki/Binding_magical_contract" title="Binding magical contract">binding magical contract</a> in place.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706181525" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter4 minerva yule ball.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706181525" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706181525" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706181525" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter4 minerva yule ball.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706181525" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter4_minerva_yule_ball.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall attending the Yule Ball and dancing with Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the year Minerva more than once exhorted her students to provide a good appearance to their guests at the castle. She attended the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with Albus Dumbledore and notably wore her hair down for the first time since Harry started his education at Hogwarts. While at the Ball, Minerva danced with both <a href="/wiki/Ludovic_Bagman" title="Ludovic Bagman">Ludovic Bagman</a> and Dumbledore, among others. In the case of the former, Harry Potter noticed Bagman kiss Minerva's hand once they had finished dancing.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva loaned <a href="/wiki/Classroom_1B" title="Classroom 1B">her classroom</a> to Harry, Ron and Hermione so they could practise spells for Harry's preparation for the Third Task. She did this after having walked in on them practising so many times around the school. At the end of the Tournament, Minerva accompanied Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> in the rescue of Harry Potter from the <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Death Eater</a> that had spent the entire school year impersonating the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, that year's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">DADA</a> professor.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall is present while Snape presents his newly activated Dark Mark</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She was instructed to guard Crouch Jnr after he revealed his part in the rebirth of Voldemort but was unable to prevent the Dementor brought by <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> from giving the Death Eater the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>. She was intensely furious at Fudge for this blunder, and severely shaken from having witnessed the unspeakably horrible act, screaming more than Harry had ever seen before. Thus, when the Minister refused to believe Dumbledore and Harry Potter about the return of Voldemort, Minerva nonetheless stood in support of her superior and her student. In the return of the Dark Lord, <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> student <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a> was carelessly murdered and a <a href="/wiki/Memorial_feast_to_Cedric_Diggory" title="Memorial feast to Cedric Diggory">memorial feast</a> was held at the end of the school year. The Second Wizarding War had now begun, despite the Ministry trying to hush up any claims of this.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Well, I think Potter and his friends ought to have fifty points apiece for alerting the world to the return of You-Know-Who! What say you, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGongall openly addressing Voldemort's return to power<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209172140" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Pheonix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190209172140" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest?cb=20190209172140" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190209172140" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Pheonix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order_of_the_Pheonix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190209172140" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Pheonix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva joins the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> had begun, Minerva joined the Order of the Phoenix and spent much of the summer of 1995 doing work for the Order. She would come and go from <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> wearing a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> dress rather than her robes, which Harry thought made her look odd. Though these duties took up much of her time, Minerva would face even greater challenges at Hogwarts. Because Dumbledore was unable to find a new professor for Defence Against the Dark Arts, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> appointed <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, a senior Ministry official and stout supporter of Fudge, to the Hogwarts staff. Minerva saw this appointment as an affront to the school itself and did little to hide her disgust.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="High_Inquisitor_at_Hogwarts">High Inquisitor at Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: High Inquisitor at Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: High Inquisitor at Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>I wonder how you expect to gain an idea of my usual teaching methods if you continue to interrupt me? You see, I do not generally permit people to talk when I am talking.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Professor McGonagall to <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> during her inspection<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102185120" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Disloyalty Minerva Dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180102185120" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102185120" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180102185120" decoding="async" width="246" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Disloyalty Minerva Dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180102185120" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva argues with <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> over Umbridge's methods of punishment</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry Potter crossed Umbridge, earning a detention in his first class with her, Minerva was sympathetic but warned him that Umbridge was not to be trifled with and that he should keep his head down. McGonagall did all she could to circumvent Umbridge's authority without risking her own security as Deputy Headmistress. Indeed, she treated Umbridge with as little credence and respect as possible while Hogwarts was under investigation by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and even gave <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> tips on how to unscrew a chandelier when he was trying to cause havoc for Umbridge. McGonagall also managed to put aside her dislike of <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a> for a time in the face of Umbridge's persecution of Hogwarts' inhabitants. It is shown she brings Trelawney back to Hogwarts after Umbridge dismissed her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Umbridge's appointment as <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">High Inquisitor</a>, Minerva was forced to endure the other woman's presence during her evaluation of Minerva's teaching. Minerva kept her temper under control, maintaining an icy exterior and yet still unleashed a dry and pointed wit on Umbridge. The encounter did serve to cheer students like <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> who heartily disliked Umbridge; Ron even expressed delight at the prospect of seeing Minerva's classes inspected, remarking that "Umbridge won't know what's hit her". Still, darker times lay ahead.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva%2C_ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180212172352" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-harry. minerva, ron.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva,_ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva%2C_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180212172352" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva%2C_ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180212172352" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva%2C_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180212172352" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-harry. minerva, ron.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva,_ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva%2C_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180212172352" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-harry._minerva,_ron.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An anxious Minerva brings Harry to  Dumbledore's Office following his vision of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>'s attack</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Minerva's best efforts to thwart the Ministry's influence at Hogwarts, things continued to grow worse. After Harry's resistance group was discovered by Umbridge, Minerva was present in Dumbledore's office when Harry was brought in. When Umbridge revealed that anti-Muggle prankster <a href="/wiki/Willy_Widdershins" title="Willy Widdershins">Willy Widdershins</a> had provided her with testimony that Harry was forming this rebel group, Minerva loudly voiced that she had wondered why he had managed to avoid prosecution for all his regurgitating toilet charges, joined in her vocal outrage by the portrait of Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Dexter_Fortescue" title="Dexter Fortescue">Dexter Fortescue</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dumbledore managed to save Harry by taking credit for the student organisation, which led to Fudge announcing his intention to arrest him and actually attempted to have him taken by force, sneering at the idea of Dumbledore taking on him and the others single-handed. Minerva, loyal to her mentor and friend, loudly declared that he wouldn't be single-handed and actually made to draw her wand, fully prepared to duel the Minister for Magic himself. She only stood down on Dumbledore's direct orders, as Hogwarts would need her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Dumbledore escaped arrest, Umbridge was appointed Headmistress over Minerva, but had virtually no support. When Umbridge invaded the career advising of the 5th-year students, Minerva finally lost her temper. During Harry Potter's session, when Umbridge kept interrupting the conversation and declaring that Harry would never be an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> at the Ministry, Minerva declared to Harry that she would help him in any way necessary to achieve his goal, even if it was the last thing she ever did. The atmosphere at Hogwarts continued to devolve under Umbridge's leadership.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="St_Mungo's_Hospital"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="St_Mungo.27s_Hospital">St Mungo's Hospital</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: St Mungo&#039;s Hospital">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: St Mungo&#039;s Hospital"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>How dare you! How </i>dare<i> you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger </b>: "<i>It's McGonagall!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>Leave him alone! Alone, I say! On what grounds are you attacking him? He has done nothing, nothing to warrant such —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; McGonagall defending Hagrid moments before she's attacked<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706044702" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva wheelchair.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20170706044702" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706044702" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20170706044702" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva wheelchair.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/Minerva_wheelchair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20170706044702" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_wheelchair.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A wheelchair bound McGonagall reading about the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> examinations, events came to a head. When <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> and several <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> attempted to evict <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> from the grounds of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Minerva sought to intervene on behalf of her colleague. Charging out of the castle, she shouted at the Aurors to leave Hagrid alone. However, before she could even draw her wand, Minerva was promptly hit with four <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a> in the chest, which required that she be moved from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> Hospital Wing to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's</a> for treatment.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hagrid was so disgusted by this attack that he attacked two of her attackers in an uncontrollable rage before fleeing, furiously denouncing them as cowards, while Madam Pomfrey said that it would be very difficult for Minerva to be hit in broad daylight. She would have resigned in protest because of this cowardly attack if the students' well-being was not placed as her priority. Many students were also outraged with this attack, to the point of ignoring their <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a> exam and even the proctor <a href="/wiki/Tofty" title="Tofty">Professor Tofty</a> expressed aloud his fury.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Hogwarts">Return to Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Return to Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Well, I think Potter and his friends ought to have fifty points apiece for alerting the world to the return of You-Know-Who — that's fifty each for Potter, the two Weasleys, Longbottom and Miss Granger. Oh — and fifty for Miss Lovegood, I suppose.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall rewards the participants of the Battle of the Department of Mysteries<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102182404" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20180102182404" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102182404" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20180102182404" decoding="async" width="241" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20180102182404" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-3808.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva going over schedules with the sixth years in 1996</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva didn't return to Hogwarts until after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. After being released from the hospital, she required the aid of a <a href="/wiki/Walking_stick" title="Walking stick">walking stick</a> for several days. Upon her return to the school, she promptly gave the six students involved in the Battle at the Ministry 50 house points each for "alerting the world to the return of You-Know-Who", in response to Snape needling Harry about Gryffindor having 0 house points.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> She also watched with some happiness when Peeves chased <a href="/wiki/Umbridge_family" title="Umbridge family">Umbridge</a> from the school, commenting that she would've joined Peeves in chasing Dolores away in the school grounds, but <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> had appropriated her walking stick.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After her recovery at St Mungo's, Minerva resumed her duties within the Order of the Phoenix as well as her teaching duties when the school year would begin again after summer.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Early in the year, she was responsible for the distribution of schedules among the the sixth year N.E.W.T. students.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Silver_and_Opals.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180720152159" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Silver and Opals.JPG" data-image-key="Silver_and_Opals.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Silver_and_Opals.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720152159" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Silver_and_Opals.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180720152159" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Silver_and_Opals.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720152159" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Silver and Opals.JPG" data-image-key="Silver_and_Opals.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Silver_and_Opals.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720152159" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Silver_and_Opals.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professors Snape and McGonagall examining a <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">cursed necklace</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva was present after <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a> was cursed by the Opal Necklace. After Harry ran off to find someone to aid Katie, he bumped into <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> and led him back to the group. After learning the nature of the event Hagrid carried Katie to the castle, accompanied by Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Leanne" title="Leanne">Leanne</a>. While in the castle Minerva appeared and asked Harry what he was holding in his hand, it was the necklace wrapped in his scarf. She then proceeded to hand over the necklace to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>, through the Caretaker <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> and questioned the the trio and Leanne on what they witnessed. Harry told her his theory that it was Draco Malfoy that gave Katie the necklace, but she scorned the theory and dismissed them. Snape was able to stop the curse from spreading any further, but Katie was taken to St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries, where she spent much of that year recovering from the effects of the <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Professor McGonagall had risen to her feet, the mournful hum in the Great Hall died away at once.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall at Albus Dumbledore's funeral<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>Later in the school year, Minerva participated in the Battle of the Astronomy Tower in 1997 after Draco sneaked Death Eaters into the school through the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>. She was stuck on the level below Harry and Dumbledore and couldn't pass on the stairs to reach them, however, Snape could (as he had the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>) and pushed past her. During the battle, Minerva duelled and personally dispatched Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>, sending her foe running for cover.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The funeral of Albus Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the battle, Minerva was devastated to learn of Snape's murder of Dumbledore, the man whom she had known nearly her entire life as a teacher, mentor and friend, and whose murderer she had let pass. After the murder was committed the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>, which was already cast into the sky, shadowed over the school grounds. After the death of Dumbledore, McGonagall held the <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">Funeral of Albus Dumbledore</a> at Hogwarts and in the final days of the school year, she took over Dumbledore's former position and became Headmistress of Hogwarts. She tried to comfort Harry about the death of Dumbledore but her efforts fell short, as she herself was devastated at the death of her beloved teacher.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Voldemort's_control_of_Hogwarts"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Voldemort.27s_control_of_Hogwarts">Voldemort's control of Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Voldemort&#039;s control of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Voldemort&#039;s control of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the war continued, Minerva remained at Hogwarts, even when it was taken over by Voldemort. This was most likely to make sure as little harm came to students, since she could act as an insider so that the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> was informed on what was going on at Hogwarts. Even when Severus was appointed Headmaster and Alecto and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> were given free rein in the school, Minerva did as much as she could to protect the students. The rebel alliance <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> founded by the students reformed and McGonagall helped to keep their meetings a secret.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You're acting on </i>Dumbledore's<i> orders? ...We shall secure the school against He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named while you search for this — this object.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall prepares for the Battle of Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>On <a href="/wiki/1_May" title="1 May">1 May</a> 1998, Minerva was present when Harry Potter, Hermione Granger, and Ron Weasley returned to Hogwarts in the middle of the night in search of <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Rowena Ravenclaw's Diadem</a>. That night, she found Amycus at the door to Ravenclaw Tower, furiously assaulting it and demanding to be let in. Dryly pointing out that perhaps his sister, whom Professor Flitwick had admitted earlier at their urgent request, could open the door and prevent him from waking half the castle. Minerva then intervened on his behalf after he told her that Alecto wasn't responding.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706050121" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-minerva 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706050121" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706050121" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706050121" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-minerva 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706050121" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-minerva_1998.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall protecting students during Snape's regime</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the door opened, they found Alecto unconscious on the floor, which Minerva surmised as the work of a Stunning Spell. Amycus then revealed that they had been warned that Harry might try to get into Ravenclaw Tower, to which Minerva responded with confusion as Harry was in her house, speaking of this with pride in her voice, before scanning the room. Amycus then horrified her by stating his plan to push the blame for Alecto summoning Voldemort on the children in the dormitories, without remorse or concern that they would likely be killed or horribly tortured. Minerva refused to allow it, prompting the Death Eater to spit in her face, only to be flung across the room with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> when Harry, who had witnessed the whole thing from under his Invisibility Cloak, revealed himself in sheer anger. With help from Harry and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, she incapacitated the Carrow siblings in the <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw_Tower" title="Ravenclaw Tower">Ravenclaw Common Room</a>. Realising that a battle was upon them, Minerva gathered <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a> and together the three Heads of House banished Severus from Hogwarts, Minerva even calling him a coward as he fled the school.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry informed McGonagall of a quest that Dumbledore had left him. In respect for Dumbledore's wishes, she offered to hold Voldemort and his army back for whilst Harry fulfilled this quest. She then proceeded to animate the castle's suits of armour and statues to help her defend the school.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Shortly before the battle, Minerva ordered Neville Longbottom with the aid of <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a> and other students to destroy the <a href="/wiki/Wooden_Bridge" title="Wooden Bridge">Wooden Bridge</a> so that the <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> could not sneak into school grounds.<sup id="cite_ref-DHF2_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHF2-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> To ensure the advantage of chaos on their side, she also ordered Argus Filch to find Peeves and bring him to her, which he did in response to her agitation.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170814145822" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva and Molly Battle og Hogwart.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170814145822" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170814145822" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170814145822" decoding="async" width="245" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva and Molly Battle og Hogwart.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170814145822" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_and_Molly_Battle_og_Hogwart.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva and Molly Weasley preparing for battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Hogwarts is threatened! Man the boundaries, protect us, do your duty to our school!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall preparing for the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After ordering the evacuation of younger students through the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>, Minerva began to help fortify the castle against the coming attack, with the assistance of her fellow teachers, Order members, and even the older students who had stayed behind to fight. When <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> suggested they take the deal offered to them by Voldemort — that of their lives in exchange for Harry Potter — Minerva ordered the cowardly girl and all those not willing to fight to leave.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva fought skillfully in the first part of the battle, during which she could have sworn she saw one of the statues that usually flanks the school's <a href="/wiki/Entrance_Gates" title="Entrance Gates">Main Gates</a> dive-bombing a cluster of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> She would later stand defiant in the lull and among many students in a crowd when Voldemort himself walked into the Hogwarts grounds. It was only when she saw Harry Potter's body being carried by Hagrid that she began to despair, letting out a scream terrible to anyone who heard it, equal to that of Ron, Hermione, and Ginny's together. Nonetheless, Minerva continued to fight when the battle resumed after the attack by the <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">Centaurs</a> on Voldemort and the Death Eaters. In the final moments of the battle, she duelled Voldemort alongside <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, though they were blasted aside by his fury when <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> was killed in a duel with <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva and other onlookers watch as Harry Potter defeats Voldemort for the final time</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall was present when Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> connected with Harry's <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> and was rebounded, signalling his final defeat at Harry's hands. She, along with everyone else in the Great Hall, hugged Harry in an uncharacteristic display of great emotion. She was one of the first to reach Harry, right behind Hermione, Ron, and Ginny. This event signalled the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> In the aftermath of the battle, Professor McGonagall brought the winged bore statue's part in the battle to the attention of <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Professor Flitwick</a>, who thought it an unlikely story seen as no one was known to have <a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">enchanted</a> them, which subsequently lead to a long-standing disagreement between the two as to whether or not the Winged Boar Statues had, in fact, participated in the Battle of Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="As_Headmistress_of_Hogwarts_(1998-)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="As_Headmistress_of_Hogwarts_.281998-.29">As Headmistress of Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1998-)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: As Headmistress of Hogwarts (1998-)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: As Headmistress of Hogwarts (1998-)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Early career"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>With the conclusion of the war, Professor McGonagall was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class, by <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> for her unwavering allegiance to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, as well as being featured on a <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Card</a>, the latter of which were an accolade she admitted she had never imagined receiving.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>  Four months later, Minerva was also officially appointed to the position of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Headmaster" title="Hogwarts Headmaster">Headmistress</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Board_of_Governors" title="Hogwarts Board of Governors">Hogwarts Board of Governors</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-MA_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MA-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> by which time the extensive damages done to the castle had been duly repaired, the <a href="/wiki/Protective_enchantment" title="Protective enchantment">protective enchantments</a> surrounding the school restored and the faculty ready to accept a new batch of <a href="/wiki/First_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="First Year">First Year</a> students for the <a href="/wiki/1998%E2%80%931999_school_year" title="1998–1999 school year">1998–1999 school year</a>. During this term, the school also guided those who would have otherwise completed their studies had it not been for the <a href="/wiki/Magic_is_Might" title="Magic is Might">Magic is Might</a> Campaign of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and his followers, such as <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a> like <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, in finishing their <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Upon assuming her new position, Minerva relocated; moving out of her sparse, stone-floored bedroom off of the <a href="/wiki/First-floor_corridor" title="First-floor corridor">first-floor corridor</a> and took up permanent residence in Professor Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Tower" title="Headmaster&#39;s Tower">old quarters</a>, whereupon her new <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Office" title="Headmaster&#39;s Office">study</a> became the home to among other things a self-playing harp, Its tones often being heard around midday, between classes.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Lost_Love_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Lost_Love-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> In the time that followed, Professor McGonagall was responsible for, among other things, finding someone to replace her as the school's Transfiguration teacher,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> finding a new, permanent replacement for the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor, the eventual employment of her former student <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Herbology_department" title="Herbology department">Herbology department</a>, under <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Herbology" title="Head of Herbology">head of department</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MA_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MA-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> whom she also eventually named her successor as <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>And while Professor McGonagall went on to become a revered and inspirational Headmistress, she could nevertheless help but notice that for years after the the Dark Lord's last stand, nearly all of their students were able to see the <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> that pulled the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_carriages" class="mw-redirect" title="Hogwarts carriages">Hogwarts carriages</a>; serving as a constant, painful reminder of the cost of said event.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> One such student was <a href="/wiki/Grim_Fawley" title="Grim Fawley">Grim Fawley</a>;  a young student in <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff House</a> whose own magical education had been marred by the loss of both his parents to the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Second_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="Second Year">Second Year</a>, the same year saw him evacuated along with most of his peers while the older students, teachers and members  <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> waged the legendary <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, which resulted in the death of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and the conclusion of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. When Fawley graduated with five <a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a> and one <a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a> on his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>., Minerva wrote him a glowing letter of recommendation for him to attach to his job application when he showed at interest in joining the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point, Minerva also tasked <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> with serving as a <a href="/wiki/Special_messenger" title="Special messenger">special messenger</a> to the family of a young <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> that had been admitted to the school, who would explain to the child's parents about the existence of magic, deliver their <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_acceptance_letter" title="Hogwarts acceptance letter">letter of acceptance</a> and take said student-to-be to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> to purchase the <a href="/wiki/Shopping_List" title="Shopping List">necessary school supplies</a>. On <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a> of that year, Professor McGonagall, who had diligently continued to collect the newcomers escorted by Professor Hagrid, even after she was in a position to delegate that task, brought the aforementioned <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_2000s_Hogwarts_student" title="Unidentified 2000s Hogwarts student">Muggle-born student</a> and the rest of the new students to the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>. Addressing the students, she held a brief speech about the importance of unity in spite of their individual differences, citing their victory at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> as a prime example of what the castle's residents may accomplish when they work together and putting at ease nervous students by reminding them that even the famous <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> had started out a student just like themselves. While overseeing the annual <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>, however, where she saw the sorting of among others <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Page" title="Daniel Page">Daniel Page</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colby_Frey" title="Colby Frey">Colby Frey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lottie_Turner" title="Lottie Turner">Lottie Turner</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robyn_Thistlethwaite" title="Robyn Thistlethwaite">Robyn Thistlethwaite</a> into their respective houses, it quickly became clear that one of the new students, a girl by the name of <a href="/wiki/Ivy_Warrington" title="Ivy Warrington">Ivy Warrington</a>, was missing from the group. After questioning their new arrivals about her whereabouts and receiving confirmation that she had indeed arrived with the rest of her peers, Professor McGonagall instructed Hagrid to set up a search party to find her, before she announced that while members of the staff searched the castle, the rest of the student body should enjoy the <a href="/wiki/Welcoming_Feast" title="Welcoming Feast">Welcoming Feast</a> while they still could, as they would have to be well-rested before embarking on the new term.<sup id="cite_ref-MA_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MA-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later that term, Professor McGonagall was occupied elsewhere when a group of First Year students snuck into her office at the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Tower" title="Headmaster&#39;s Tower">Headmistress' Tower</a> to use the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Pensieve" title="Hogwarts Pensieve">pensieve</a> to view a <a href="/wiki/Memory" title="Memory">memory</a> that had been contained within the locket of <a href="/wiki/Ivy_Warrington" title="Ivy Warrington">Ivy Warrington</a>, and as such presumably unaware of their intrusion until afterwards. In light of her mysterious disappearance at the beginning of the term, however, Professor McGonagall had reached out to Ivy's family to keep them informed on the situation, and eventually got in touch with Miss Warrington's <a href="/wiki/Warrington_sisters%27_grandmother" title="Warrington sisters&#39; grandmother">grandmother</a>, whom she invited to the castle so she could help shred light on the reason behind Ivy's erratic behaviour and apparent memory loss. Sympathetic to the difficulty of Madam Warrington's position in deciding to <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">modify</a> the memory of her own grandchild to spare her the pain of knowing that she had accidentally <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">vanished</a> her own sister, she commended the old witch for her good intentions and assured her that in spite of everything, Ivy had underwent a tremendous amount of personal growth over the course of her first term, expressing the opinion that she and the group of friends she had made had a bright future ahead of them.<sup id="cite_ref-MA_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MA-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2008" title="2008">2008</a>, Minerva gave <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who had since joined the Ministry and risen to a high-placed office in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a>, permission for Dumbledore's old notes on <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i> to be published as part of her new translation of the book.<sup id="cite_ref-TBB_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBB-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Calamity">The Calamity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Calamity">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: The Calamity"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 117px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200828111926" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="115" height="381" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brilliant Minerva McGonagall WU.png" data-image-key="Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/115?cb=20200828111926" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png/revision/latest?cb=20200828111926" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/115?cb=20200828111926" decoding="async" width="115" height="381" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brilliant Minerva McGonagall WU.png" data-image-key="Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/115?cb=20200828111926" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brilliant_Minerva_McGonagall_WU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Headmistress McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Assisting_the_SOS_Task_Force">Assisting the SOS Task Force</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Assisting the SOS Task Force">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Assisting the SOS Task Force"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Following the outbreak of the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a> and the establishment of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a>, several faculty members at Hogwarts was happy to lend them a hand in addressing the catastrophe. While their old <a href="/wiki/Charms_Master" title="Charms Master">Charms Master</a> was used his past as an expert on martial magic to assist in the training of prospective <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a>, Minerva on her part became involved in the tutelage of <a href="/wiki/Calamity_Investigator" title="Calamity Investigator">Calamity Investigators</a> wishing pursued a career as a <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a>. And though she expressed pleasure when such members showed an interest in joining their ranks, she still warned them of the difficulties they would have to face along the way, as well as the fact that they might be called upon to do things they never thought possible. She welcomed them by giving them a copy of the letters that were once exchanged between <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Adalbert_Waffling" title="Adalbert Waffling">Adalbert Waffling</a> to help improve their skills in addressing the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a>, specifically in fighting Impaired Foes. She also taught them the <a href="/wiki/Deterioration_Hex" title="Deterioration Hex">Deterioration Hex</a> for purpose of impairing their foes and instructed them on the proper stances to cast a far more powerful <a href="/wiki/Protection_Charm" title="Protection Charm">Protection Charm</a>; to the point of enchanting a teammate along with sessions to improve their attention for details and gave them a lesson on how to best use the strength of allies in battle and visiting to give a personal discourse on how to combat Curiosities.<sup id="cite_ref-Wizards_Unite_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wizards_Unite-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Calamity_surge_at_Hogwarts">Calamity surge at Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Calamity surge at Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Calamity surge at Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Shortly prior to the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%932020_school_year" title="2019–2020 school year">2019–2020 school year</a>, the Headmistress received owls from no less than three students in <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw House</a> asking if they could receive their lesson plans early as not to fall behind in their studies, an exchange she noted that it was not uncommon for her to have with students of that house at the beginning of each term; noting that most students would be excited by the idea of an extended holiday.
