Around the same time, she also unsuccessfully tried to talk a highly talented student in <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a> out of transferring to <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a>, where the she felt they would be safer seen as The Calamity was apparently targeting her house.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>When the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> was whisked away by The Calamity just shortly prior to its scheduled departure on <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a>, she quickly solicited the assistance of a reputable member of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">SOS Task Force</a> that <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> had recommended, hoping said individual could returned the train in time for the new school year. In the meantime, however,  due to the ongoing surge, a number of <a href="/wiki/Foundable" title="Foundable">Foundables</a> materialised on the school grounds, including <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Werewolves</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fire-breathing_chicken" title="Fire-breathing chicken">Fire-breathing chickens</a>, expressing the concern that lest the Calamity was not dealt with, she would have to spend the entire school term keeping <a href="/wiki/First_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="First Year">First Year</a> <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> away from them. Professor McGonagall was also surprised to discover, and took no small amount of pride in, the fact that more than seventy-four percent of the volunteers that had taken time off their busy schedules to assist the Ministry of Magic - by quill and parchment - with the arduous job of tracking, sorting, cataloguing, collating, and archiving returned <a href="/wiki/Foundable" title="Foundable">Foundables</a> for the Ministry were current and former members of <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff House</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Calamity_Investigator" title="Calamity Investigator">Calamity Investigator</a> was eventually successful in returning the Hogwarts Express in time for the start of the term, much to the relief of Minerva; who pointed out that the time-honoured tradition of riding the train to school was as much part of the "Hogwarts experience" as the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>. She was also relieved to hear of the safe return of the <a href="/wiki/Trolley_witch" title="Trolley witch">Trolley witch</a>, who had been turned into a <a href="/wiki/Foundable" title="Foundable">Foundable</a> and at some point afterwards retrieved by the aforementioned Task Force member, saying that the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> would not be the same without her and her sweets, noting that she could remember her working at the train even back when Minerva herself was a student, during which she was "partial" to her <a href="/wiki/Pumpkin_Pasty" title="Pumpkin Pasty">Pumpkin Pasties</a>. That was not to say that her troubles was over, however, as The Calamity hit the school itself next, spiriting off with the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> in Hogwart's <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Thestral_herd" title="Hogwarts Thestral herd">herd</a>, one of their <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_carriages" class="mw-redirect" title="Hogwarts carriages">carriages</a>, one of their <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_boats" title="Hogwarts boats">boats</a>, a Winged Boar Statue and even the sign directing people between <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade Village</a>; all of which the same diligent individual was able to retrieve and return to their allotted places, much to the delight of the denizens of Hogwarts Castle. Upon thanking their saviour, the Headmistress informed them that the school had suffered no lasting effects from the recent outburst of the Calamity, not counting the students' new favourite excuse for nothing finishing their schoolwork in time; 'the Calamity stole my homework!'<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts_18-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Back_to_Hogwarts-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Lost_Love">The Lost Love</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Lost Love">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: The Lost Love"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Later on during the term, Professor McGonagall reached out to the same individual that had done such an exemplary job helping the school earlier that school year, informing them that the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a> had spirited away with quite a few of items of a "personal and private nature", soliciting their assistance in getting them back. Along on this endeavour was one of her former students and fellow Head of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a>, <a href="/wiki/Constance_Pickering" title="Constance Pickering">Constance Pickering</a>, who kept commenting and asking questions about each of the artefacts as they were retrieved, much to the dismay of the Headmistress. The first possession to be returned to her self-playing harp, at which point Minerva showed signs of mild exasperation when she had to explain to Miss Pickering that the self-playing instrument had, as the name suggests, been bewitched to play itself. The next items on the list was the <a href="/wiki/Memory" title="Memory">memory</a> of a <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_hornbill" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s hornbill">hornbill</a> that she once owned, which she had used as a teaching aid during her career as a <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> professor, and remembered it fondly as "a good bird", although she had not viewed it as a pet, as she was more partial to cats. The next items on the list included a school crest and her <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class, which she had framed and kept in her office, and an old photo of <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">Dougal McGregor</a>, about whom she refused to comment when Pickering questioned the man's identity, saying only that he was "<i>a man [she} once knew</i>" and that that was all she was prepared to say on the matter.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Lost_Love_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Lost_Love-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When all of the items had been retrieved, she mildly admonished Miss Pickering for prying into her personal life, noting that she had a keen and inquisitive mind, but that she nevertheless needed to learn that she did not have the right to the answer of every question just because she asks.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Lost_Love_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Lost_Love-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inter-House_Cup">Inter-House Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Inter-House Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Inter-House Cup"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>When the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a> made another surge near the end of the always much anticipated Inter-House Quidditch League and whisked away with among other things the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Hogwarts Quidditch Cup</a>, Minerva alerted the Ministry of Magic, which duly dispatched a member of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> to return them all. One of the <a href="/wiki/Foundable" title="Foundable">Foundables</a> in question was an old <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2000" title="Nimbus 2000">Nimbus 2000</a>, prompting a <a href="/wiki/Chaser" title="Chaser">Chaser</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> to grow concerned that her broom, which of the same model, might vanish and be weakened if the same happened to hers, only for the Headmistress to assure her that the broom in question was almost certainly the echo of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Nimbus_2000" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Nimbus 2000">the one</a> that once belonged to another, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">famous student</a> that played on their team as well. When the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house ghost, <a href="/wiki/Sir_Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington" class="mw-redirect" title="Sir Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington">Sir Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington</a>, was spirited away along with the cup and turned him into a Foundable, Minerva was delighted to see his safe return, stating that she had meant to ask his opinion on the Calamity, seen as how he, being somewhat separated from his original self, just like the Foundables were, perhaps had some interesting insights into the Calamity they had not considered.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_HQC_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_HQC-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2019_onwards">2019 onwards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 2019 onwards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 2019 onwards"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160608003121" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg" data-image-key="RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608003121" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160608003121" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608003121" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg" data-image-key="RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608003121" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:RoseInGreatHallCursedChild.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva watching <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose Granger-Weasley</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p> Minerva was also a staple in the Wizarding community and often attended Extraordinary General Meetings, most notably the meeting in 2020 where they discussed the concerning movement of Voldemort's allies. Furthermore, Minerva also revealed that someone had taken <a href="/wiki/Boomslang_skin" title="Boomslang skin">Boomslang skin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lacewing_fly" title="Lacewing fly">lacewing flies</a> from the Potions stores during the summer break, the ingredients for <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Assisting_Albus_Potter">Assisting Albus Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Assisting Albus Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Assisting Albus Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> did not arrive at Hogwarts, Minerva sent owls to their parents and later met with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and her husband <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, to find them. Minerva even suggested having <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Professor Longbottom</a> aid them, due to his expertise in <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> being useful in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harryandminerva.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20190707214903" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="238" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harryandminerva.jpeg" data-image-key="Harryandminerva.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harryandminerva.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20190707214903" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harryandminerva.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20190707214903" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harryandminerva.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20190707214903" decoding="async" width="238" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harryandminerva.jpeg" data-image-key="Harryandminerva.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harryandminerva.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20190707214903" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harryandminerva.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> arguing over <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a>'s friendship</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>After Albus and Scorpius meddled in time and made it so Ron and Hermione never married, Albus was <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> and Ron married <a href="/wiki/Padma_Patil" title="Padma Patil">Padma Patil</a>, Minerva was still Headmistress of Hogwarts. She tried to advise Harry on interfering in Albus and Scorpius's friendship, but he insisted on keeping them separated and blackmailed Minerva into using the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> to keep them apart.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>  
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190519074317" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall marauders map.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190519074317" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190519074317" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190519074317" decoding="async" width="220" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall marauders map.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190519074317" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall_marauders_map.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva examines the <a href="/wiki/Marauder%27s_Map" title="Marauder&#39;s Map">Marauder's Map</a> with <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>But, after using the map a few times and once purposefully ignoring the two because they were under the Invisibility Cloak, Minerva was again visited by Harry, Ginny and Draco and told him that she wanted no part in ruining friendships, to which he apologised and begged that she use the map to find Albus and Scorpius so that he can apologise to him too. Minerva used the map to discover that they were in the <a href="/wiki/Moaning_Myrtle%27s_Bathroom" title="Moaning Myrtle&#39;s Bathroom">girls' bathroom on the first floor</a>. Minerva and the parents tried to find them, but <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Moaning Myrtle</a> reveals that they used a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to save <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>, much to Minerva's shock.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_29-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Albus and Scorpius returned to the <a href="/wiki/Alternate_reality" title="Alternate reality">original timeline</a>, Minerva found them and they confessed what they had done. Minerva invited <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> to meet with her and she reminded them that although Albus and Scorpius were being noble, their meddling had returned them to the darkest times of the wizarding war and to never forget that their current peaceful world had been created because of the sacrifices of those who lost their lives. She then ordered them to find the missing Time-Turner.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_29-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>The door swung open at once. A tall, black-haired witch in emerald-green robes stood there. She had a very stern face and Harry's first thought was that she was not someone to cross.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry Potter's first impression of McGonagall<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810173547" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="217" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PromoHP1 Minerva McGonagall 2.jpg" data-image-key="PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150810173547" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810173547" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150810173547" decoding="async" width="165" height="217" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PromoHP1 Minerva McGonagall 2.jpg" data-image-key="PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150810173547" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PromoHP1_Minerva_McGonagall_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was said to be a tall, rather severe-looking, and "sprightly" seventy-year-old woman. She had black hair which was rarely let down, and the majority of the time was combed back into a tight bun.<sup id="cite_ref-Hair_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hair-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In her youth, Minerva was described to not be as beautiful as her <a href="/wiki/Isobel_Ross" title="Isobel Ross">mother</a>, but she was still rather pretty according to her picture in that age.  
</p><p>Minerva always had a very prim expression. She also was known for her mouth to become very thin whenever she was angry. <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> Potter made analogies to McGonagall looking like she was going to explode, breathe fire and shoot sparks from her nose based on how transparent her anger could appear. When Minerva was happy or relaxed, she seemed like a different person entirely. She was capable of blending into <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> crowds though Harry noted that the appearance didn't suit her.
</p><p>Minerva often wore emerald green robes or her favourite tartan pattern. She wore square spectacles that matched the markings around the eyes of her <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>: a silver tabby cat. She also wore a pointed hat cocked to one side. As Minerva was a fan of tartan print and would often wear it to <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> games along with a woolly hat covering her ears. 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i><a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Moody</a>, we never use <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Discipline_at_Hogwarts" title="Discipline at Hogwarts">punishment</a>! Surely Professor Dumbledore told you that?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva's strict but fair attitude as an educator<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 158px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/McGeee.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20081205172219" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="156" height="257" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="McGeee.PNG" data-image-key="McGeee.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/McGeee.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20081205172219" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/McGeee.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20081205172219" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/McGeee.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20081205172219" decoding="async" width="156" height="257" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="McGeee.PNG" data-image-key="McGeee.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/McGeee.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20081205172219" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:McGeee.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva smiling at the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, a rare occurrence</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva almost constantly exuded magnanimity and sternness, being held in great respect (and some fear) by nearly all students and staff. Used to having her way, she tolerated neither audacity nor silliness from her pupils and was known to turn cold towards people who said or did things in front of her that were stupid, or if she thought they were trying to be funny.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She was a woman who rarely smiled or gave compliments freely. Despite her stern demeanour, Minerva did exhibit a dry sense of humour which usually came out when times were tough. She wasn't afraid to speak her mind and showed quite a sharp tongue, especially during arguments.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>We teachers are rather good at magic, you know. I am sure we will be able to hold him off for a while if we all put our best efforts into it. Of course, something will have to be done about Professor Snape –</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva's fierce dedication to protecting Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>True to Gryffindor, Minerva valued bravery and courage highly, believing cowardice be a heavy flaw. She fought the Death Eaters and protected her students, proving her bravery. Despite her loyalty to her house, Minerva was a fair-minded person who was known for docking points from students in her own House when she saw it must be done.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Although she permitted of-age students to choose whether they wanted  to stay or evacuate for the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> as a respect for their valour and rights, she gave the strict orders for anyone underage to evacuate, prioritising their safety over their courage and refusing to let under-qualified children risk  dying in battle despite their desires.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For the most part, though, Minerva usually maintained great emotional composure, without being indifferent. Although she wasn't always particularly personable, she could be very warm and supportive during times of trouble or loss and cared a great deal about her students, both personally and academically. She was known to be extremely caring in times of tragedy, being known for her kindness in her own reserved manner. Though it rarely happened, Minerva showed a temper that could reveal itself on occasions when she was angry or flustered.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Apparently, she shared this temper with her father. Upon seeing Harry's alleged death, Minerva screamed in such despair that Harry never heard before.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Professor McGonagall, who could spot trouble quicker than any teacher in the school, was there in a flash.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva's keen perceptiveness as a Hogwarts teacher<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>As the devoted instructor of <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration classes</a>, Minerva highly respected this <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">specific branch</a> of magic, which she considered  be among the most difficult and sophisticated magic that Hogwarts students learn.  She become an <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> - a complicated, long process- to further her study in this subject and enjoyed correcting articles in <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_Today" title="Transfiguration Today">Transfiguration Today</a>. On the other hand, Minerva had very little patience for the field of <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, due to its impreciseness and rarity of true Seers.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though she gave up Quidditch on leaving Hogwarts, the innately competitive Minerva later took a keen interest in the fortunes of her house team and retained a keen eye for Quidditch talent. She enjoyed watching <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>, and supported the <a href="/wiki/Montrose_Magpies" title="Montrose Magpies">Montrose Magpies</a>.
</p><p>Minerva inherited her cast-iron moral sense from her father. As a law-abiding citizen, she respected the particular law that all Animagi of Britain must register, insisting that <a href="/wiki/Talbott_Winger" title="Talbott Winger">Talbott Winger</a> do so despite understanding his reason of secrecy. She wasn't inducted into the Order of the Phoenix during Voldemort’s first climb to power because the Order was held as a renegade outfit by the Ministry, who feared Dumbledore’s charisma and magical talent and were inclined to harbour fears that he wished to succeed them. Instead, she became their informant and bravely spied on Voldemort's followers in the guise of a cat.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, by the time of the second wizarding war, Minerva was no longer prepared to act as a spy for a Ministry she believed had become corrupt and dangerous. She is known to have a very severe dislike and hatred of those who abuse power, such as her making an enemy of <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> for the latter's bigoted and sociopathic behaviour. This also displayed her own distaste for racial prejudice and sadism.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Following the confrontation with the Death Eaters who had invaded Hogwarts at the time of Albus Dumbledore’s death, Minerva became a fully fledged member of the Order of the Phoenix, which was now, more than ever, seen as an outlaw organisation. Similarly, she stood up to <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a>, despite the Death Eater's higher authority at the time, refusing to let him blame the students for <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto's</a> blunder and looked down at him with pure disgust.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In her free-time, Minerva was known to enjoy needlework.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>Minerva was a gifted Transfiguration student to say the least. But it's been most satisfying to see her grow into a master of magic as well.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> on Minerva's outstanding magical prowess<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 158px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Patronus_Cat2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170109001359" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="156" height="192" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Patronus Cat2.jpg" data-image-key="Patronus_Cat2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Patronus_Cat2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20170109001359" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Patronus_Cat2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170109001359" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Patronus_Cat2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20170109001359" decoding="async" width="156" height="192" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Patronus Cat2.jpg" data-image-key="Patronus_Cat2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Patronus_Cat2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20170109001359" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Patronus_Cat2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva McGonagall's Patronus, a cat</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was an incredibly powerful and talented <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a> whom none should have ever underestimated. Her magical prowess allowed her to be the teacher of <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a>, a remarkably complex field of magic which she proved to be an expert in. She was also highly capable in many areas of magic as well as Transfiguration, the proof of this being she survived both Wizarding Wars and a duel with Voldemort himself, as well as correctly brewing the extremely advanced Animagus potion at only seventeen years of age. She was also the only person ever seen to produce three Patronus charms at once, which she additionally did non-verbally. Many wizards and witches alike are unable to produce one Patronus whilst saying the incantation, so this is further evidence of Minerva's world class ability. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>Professor McGonagall is the most powerful witch I know.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> on Minerva's outstanding magical prowess<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> mastery</b>: Minerva was an exceptionally powerful and talented witch, having inherited such talent from her mother and great-grandmother. She achieved top grades in her <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.Ls</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.Ts</a> when she was at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_school_of_witchcraft_and_wizardry" class="mw-redirect" title="Hogwarts school of witchcraft and wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, being quickly recognised as the most outstanding student of her year, with a particular talent for <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>. During her school years, she was the recipient of several awards such as the "<i>Transfiguration Today</i> Most Promising Newcomer Award". As an adult, Minerva displayed her tremendous skills and powers by successfully becoming the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Transfiguration" title="Head of Transfiguration">Head of Transfiguration</a>, Deputy Headmistress, and Headmistress at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry along with surviving both Wizarding Wars and even going on to challenge Voldemort himself along with Horace Slughorn and Kingsley Shacklebolt at the very end of the second wizarding war.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">nonverbal magic</a></b>: Minerva was shown to be extremely skilful at non-verbal magic for a wide variety of spells, especially transfiguration spells and charms which she could perform with just a wave of her wand. This is a testament to her formidable magical skills as both these branches of magic are difficult to begin with not to mention to do them non verbally which requires intense concentration and focus. She could even perform certain spells intentionally without her wand, such as the <a href="/wiki/Avifors_spell" class="mw-redirect" title="Avifors spell">Avifors spell</a> and often wandlessly conjured a textbook into her hands during Transfiguration class.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> She stalemated and gained the upper hand over Severus Snape in a fierce duel without uttering a single incantation which is further evidence of her extraordinary skills - lesser witches and wizards seemed to produce weaker magic when using non-verbal spells or under the influence of Silencing Charms, but she seemed unhindered. She was fully capable of disintegrating Snape's fiery serpent he sent at her with just a wave of her wand and instantly turning it into swarm of daggers without saying the incantation. They were so powerful even without the incantation that he was forced to hide behind a suit of armour. She non-verbally untransfigured Draco Malfoy when he was turned into a ferret by simply pointing her wand at him.  When Neville Longbottom vanished one of the legs of his desk by accident during a lesson, she had it back very shortly after with just a wave of her wand. She also non-verbally <a href="/wiki/Silver_rope_conjuring_spell" title="Silver rope conjuring spell">conjured a length of shimmering silver rope</a> to hang the Carrow siblings before the Battle of Hogwarts to incapacitate them.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>As if one of them could have Stunned Minerva McGonagall face-on by daylight!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a> on Minerva's exceptional duelling capabilities<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 279px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110716140837" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="277" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/277?cb=20110716140837" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110716140837" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/277?cb=20110716140837" decoding="async" width="277" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/277?cb=20110716140837" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall duelling Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Minerva was an immensely skilful duellist. She was described as moving "faster than <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> Potter would have believed", displaying an incredible amount of speed and precision with her spell work. Though she was hit by four <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunning spells</a> without warning by a group of <a href="/wiki/Three_Aurors_who_tried_to_arrest_Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Three Aurors who tried to arrest Rubeus Hagrid">Aurors</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a> furiously insisted that they wouldn't have stood a chance in an actual fight.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, Minerva easily overpowered <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a> even when she had aid from <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">her brother</a>, sending them desperately escaping from her spells, and survived the battle unscathed.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> In 1998, shortly before the Battle of Hogwarts, she proved herself capable of not only matching <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> in a fierce duel, quickly and easily countering all of his spells and responding with her own, but she also managed to begin to gain the upper hand sending daggers so powerful after him that he was forced to take refuge behind a shield of armour when he couldn't counter her spell. With aid from Pomona Sprout and Filius Flitwick, she swiftly forced Snape to flee from the school by jumping out of a classroom window and flying through the grounds. Even without them, her ability to make Snape unable to counter one of her spells showed Minerva alone could have probably eventually defeated Snape (although it must also be noted that Snape wasn't fighting to kill her). Minerva emerged as one of the survivors of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and most likely defeated many Death Eaters given her previous results in duels. Alongside <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, she even duelled <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> himself to a stalemate and they were only overpowered when Voldemort's rage of Bellatrix's death caused his magic to explode, although it must be noted that Voldemort was wielding the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> at the time without having achieved mastery over it and Harry's <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">loving sacrifice</a> was weakening the power of Voldemort's spells.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Her duelling knowledge remained even as she grew older, with her instructing members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> how to improve their sight and teamwork.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
