<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Professor McGonagall raised her wand again and pointed it at Snape’s desk. A large plate of sandwiches, two silver goblets, and a jug of iced pumpkin juice appeared with a pop.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva making food and drink appear with transfiguration<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120814192903" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="89" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="COS Vera Verto demo.gif" data-image-key="COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120814192903" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120814192903" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120814192903" decoding="async" width="220" height="89" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="COS Vera Verto demo.gif" data-image-key="COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120814192903" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:COS_Vera_Verto_demo.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva transforming a <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">bird</a> into a water goblet, using the spell <i><a href="/wiki/Vera_Verto" title="Vera Verto">Vera Verto</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Minerva was taught <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> by Albus Dumbledore, showing a particular talent in the subject even at a young age despite coming to consider her subject to be among the most complex and dangerous magic taught at Hogwarts. With guidance from her teacher Albus Dumbledore, she was skilled enough to achieve the <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> transformation at the young age of seventeen. Her record was so impressive that she earned the aforementioned Transfiguration Today Most Promising Newcomer Award. Her knowledge and mastery would grow to the point that she managed to do a good enough of a job as a member of that department that she effectively assumed the position of Head of Transfiguration after Dumbledore (who seemed to be her only superior around the time) became Headmaster.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Minerva was therefore extremely accomplished in all branches of transfiguration, including <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">Conjuration</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">Vanishment</a>, <a href="/wiki/Transformation" title="Transformation">Transformation</a> and <a href="/wiki/Untransfiguration" title="Untransfiguration">Untransfiguration</a>. Due to her mastery of this magic, Minerva was one of the teachers trusted to protect the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, which she did magnificently by enlarging an <a href="/wiki/Chessboard_Chamber" title="Chessboard Chamber">entire set of chess</a> to giant size and making them alive. Some of her spells included transforming her <a href="/wiki/Desk_Into_Pig" title="Desk Into Pig">desk into a pig</a> and then <a href="/wiki/Untransfiguration" title="Untransfiguration">reversed</a> this transformation in 1991.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In 1992, when Harry and Ron had to eat in Snape's office, she transfigured a <a href="/wiki/Endless_Sandwiches" title="Endless Sandwiches">plate of sandwiches</a> that would automatically refill itself and a fan to "waft" <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington" title="Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington">Nearly Headless Nick</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> She was the one to reverse the transfiguration spell <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> (disguised as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>) used to turn <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> into a ferret in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> In 1998, Minerva tied up <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">the</a> <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Carrows</a> by conjuring a silver rope and a net as restraints. In her duel with Snape, she easily turned the snake that he had turned the rope she launched at him into into a cloud of smoke, which she subsequently transformed into a <a href="/wiki/Smoke_into_daggers_spell" title="Smoke into daggers spell">flurry of daggers</a> which Snape was forced to avoid by hiding behind a suit of armour.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/McGonagall_Animagus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140626203039" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="McGonagall Animagus.gif" data-image-key="McGonagall_Animagus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/McGonagall_Animagus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626203039" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/McGonagall_Animagus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140626203039" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/McGonagall_Animagus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626203039" decoding="async" width="245" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="McGonagall Animagus.gif" data-image-key="McGonagall_Animagus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/McGonagall_Animagus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140626203039" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:McGonagall_Animagus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall Animagus transformation</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Really, what has got into you all today? Not that it matters, but that’s the first time my transformation’s not got applause from a class.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva to <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a> students in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, regarding her impressive abilities as an Animagus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a></b>: Minerva learned how to become an Animagus under Dumbledore's tutelage during her time as a student at Hogwarts, transforming into a tabby cat at will. She often used this ability when she didn't wish to be recognised. An example of this usage was when she spied on the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursley family</a> before Dumbledore brought Harry to them.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> On his notes of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>, Dumbledore stated that Minerva asked him to explain that she had never abused the ability for any surreptitious purposes, setting aside legitimate business for the Order of the Phoenix (and previously the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>) where secrecy and concealment were imperative to survive and get information from the enemy. Minerva demonstrated her transformation to the students in their <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a>, which usually got applause. When Hermione Granger searched for Animagus references in her third year, she saw that her Professor was one of the few registered Animagi in the 20th century.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 301px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Piertotum_Locomotor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822060753" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="299" height="148" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Piertotum Locomotor.gif" data-image-key="Piertotum_Locomotor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Piertotum_Locomotor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/299?cb=20160822060753" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Piertotum_Locomotor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822060753" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Piertotum_Locomotor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/299?cb=20160822060753" decoding="async" width="299" height="148" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Piertotum Locomotor.gif" data-image-key="Piertotum_Locomotor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Piertotum_Locomotor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/299?cb=20160822060753" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Piertotum_Locomotor.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall bringing the suits of armour to life</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>From the tip burst three silver cats with spectacle markings around their eyes.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva conjuring three consecutive Patronuses with her wand<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Minerva was shown to be incredibly skilled in charm-work. She was effortlessly capable of performing many simple everyday charms non-verbally without fail, such as the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mending_Charm" title="Mending Charm">Mending Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wand-Lighting_Charm" title="Wand-Lighting Charm">Wand-Lighting Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Freezing_Spell" title="Freezing Spell">Freezing Spell</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-LEGOY1_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEGOY1-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTPG_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPG-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>, and <a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Levitation Charm</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> She was also able to successfully teach her students various charms related to transfiguration such as the <a href="/wiki/Colour_Change_Charm" title="Colour Change Charm">Colour Change Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mending_Charm" title="Mending Charm">Mending Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hardening_Charm" title="Hardening Charm">Hardening Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bird-Conjuring_Charm" title="Bird-Conjuring Charm">Bird-Conjuring Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Softening_Charm" title="Softening Charm">Softening Charm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Revelio_Charm" title="Revelio Charm">Revelio Charm</a> in her classes.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Minerva had mastered the <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, being able to create a powerful corporeal Patronus in the form of a <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">cat</a> — identical to her Animagus — , being the only person seen to cast three Patronuses at once. She also was able to use her Patronus as a means of communication, as taught to her by Dumbledore. Minerva was also proficient in the use of the <i><a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">Piertotum Locomotor</a></i> charm, describing it as one of the spells she best excelled in and favoured, using it to such a great effect that with a single use, she animated virtually all of the thousands of desks and suits of armour in order to defend Hogwarts during the final battle with Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> She was also able to perform a powerful <a href="/wiki/Amplifying_Charm" title="Amplifying Charm">Amplifying Charm</a>, which was capable of being heard across the castle, using it to summon the other Professors to the <a href="/wiki/Second-floor_corridor" title="Second-floor corridor">second-floor corridor</a> when the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Heir of Slytherin</a> took a student into the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS16_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS16-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Minerva was exceptionally experienced and accomplished in defensive magic as she fought in the two wizarding wars and survived, having defeated powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_wizard" class="mw-redirect" title="Dark wizard">dark wizards</a> and witches in process and even surviving a duel with Voldemort himself.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> During her early years in teaching, Minerva effortlessly <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">undid</a> the effects of the <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charm</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Oscausi" title="Oscausi">Oscausi</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> placed on a Gryffindor girl.<sup id="cite_ref-COGS_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COGS-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> While not as powerful as her predecessor, it was nevertheless the case that Minerva, upon being appointed Headmistress of Hogwarts by the Board of Governors, as all those that had held the post before her, was charged with handling the protective enchantments surrounding the school, which, considering her still considerable abilities, she likely still did so very well. She was able to teach how to greatly increase the strength of the Protection Charm of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Before Harry or Luna could act, Professor McGonagall rose to her feet, pointed her wand at the groggy Death Eater, and said, “Imperio”. Amycus got up, walked over to his sister, picked up her wand, then shuffled obediently to Professor McGonagall and handed it over along with his own.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;A rare example of Minerva using an Unforgivable Curse<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Whilst she did not practise the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, Minerva was surprisingly capable in the field. She was able to successfully cast an effective <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a> on <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> a remarkable feat as the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a> require both heartfelt intent and power in order to be effectively cast. She seemed to have no trouble performing standard <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a>, casting the spell <i><a href="/wiki/Oscausi" title="Oscausi">Oscausi</a></i> on the <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_Gryffindor_girl_2_(1910%27s)" class="mw-redirect" title="Unidentified Gryffindor girl 2 (1910&#39;s)">girl</a> who had had it cast previously on her by Leta<sup id="cite_ref-COGS_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COGS-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a> in a failed attempt to free <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> (openly noting she used it when it was previously unleashed upon the school successfully).<sup id="cite_ref-HM_13-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> She was particularly proficient in the use of <a href="/wiki/Deterioration_Hex" title="Deterioration Hex">Deterioration Hex</a>, enough so to teach them to the members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>She brandished her wand at a touch on the wall and it flew out of its bracket. Harry, about to curse Snape, was forced to pull Luna out of the way of the descending flames, which became a ring of fire that filled the corridor and flew like a lasso at Snape.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall non-verbally and easily filling the corridor with fire in her duel with Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b>Elemental magic aptitude</b>: Much like her mentor, Dumbledore, Minerva seemed to be exceptionally capable with manipulating <a href="/wiki/Fire" title="Fire">fire</a>. When freeing <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a>, she along with Snape were able to free him with the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a> while avoiding burning his flesh. When duelling the extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, she easily manipulated the fire from the torches into a fiery whirlwind first and easily blasted to smoke the fiery serpent he transformed her attack into.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: During her school years at Hogwarts, Minerva was a skilful player of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>. However, while playing, she suffered a number of serious injuries — such as a concussion and broken bones— that forced her to give up playing. It is highly possible that the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> had cheated in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Minerva had very advanced abilities in brewing potions, as she was capable of brewing the <a href="/wiki/Animagus_potion" title="Animagus potion">Animagus potion</a>, which was known to be immensely difficult, complex and time-consuming with great consequences if brewed incorrectly,<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> showing her superior talent in potion-making.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a></b>: Minerva was highly proficient and well versed in the study of Ancient Runes or Runology, being able to understand and translate complex <a href="/wiki/Rune" title="Rune">runic</a> scriptures, alphabets and symbols correctly, often using the help of a highly useful and practical <a href="/wiki/Rune_Dictionary" title="Rune Dictionary">Rune Dictionary</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-LEGOY1_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEGOY1-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LHP5-7_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LHP5-7-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Control of <a href="/wiki/Underage_magic" title="Underage magic">Underage magic</a></b>: As an infant, Minerva had early signs of magic. She inadvertently <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">summoned</a> toys that had been left on upper shelves to her cot, made the <a href="/wiki/McGonagalls%27_cat" title="McGonagalls&#39; cat">family cat</a> do her bidding, and her <a href="/wiki/Robert_McGonagall_Snr%27s_bagpipes" title="Robert McGonagall Snr&#39;s bagpipes">father's bagpipes</a> play themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Further evidence of her staggering magical ability was that the only other person known to be able to control animals as a child was none other than Voldemort himself.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Intellectual giftedness</b>: McGonagall was an incredibly wise, observant, and intelligent witch. She was once given the option to become a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a>, though she turned it down in preference for Gryffindor, with her officially becoming a known <a href="/wiki/Hatstall" title="Hatstall">Hatstall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> In 1998, she effortlessly solved the riddle to allow <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw_Tower" title="Ravenclaw Tower">Ravenclaw Tower</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Minerva's strategical-sense and deduction skills, along with her cautious nature, were shown several times: She confiscated Harry's <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> to be "examined" because she correctly guessed it to have been sent by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> (though she did this because she incorrectly believed it was lethally cursed),<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> did all she could to circumvent <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s authority without risking her own security as Deputy Headmistress for certain time and gave <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> tips when he was trying to cause havoc for Umbridge;<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and helped to keep the meetings of the reformed Dumbledore's Army a secret.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Shortly before the final battle, Minerva ordered her students, with the aid of <a href="/wiki/Pyrotechnics" title="Pyrotechnics">explosive magic</a>, to destroy the main access to Hogwarts so the <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> could not sneak into school grounds<sup id="cite_ref-DHF2_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHF2-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> and ordered the <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">caretaker</a> to find Peeves to ensure the advantage of chaos on their side.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Hogwarts needs you, Minerva!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore trusting Minerva to run the school just before temporarily going on the run.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b>Leadership skills</b>: Minerva was an exceptionally effective leader, being able to take charge in any situation within minutes. During the long absences of Dumbledore, she was the one to step in to fill his shoes.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In the upstart of the Battle of Hogwarts, Minerva took charge of the school and secure it against Voldemort and his Death Eaters. She led the defenders of Hogwarts during the battle with great efficiency, persisting against the forces of darkness even at the face of so many casualties in the first round of battle before turning the tides with additional help and ultimately coming out victorious when Harry defeated Voldemort once and for all.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> After everything returned to normal, Minerva became the permanent Headmistress of Hogwarts. Her leadership skills would help her when she became the leader of the members of the newly created <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who desired to become a Professor, being able to lead both those under her charge and her fellow instructors into fighting the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a> while remaining hidden from <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Physical aptitude</b>: It should be noted that Minerva was in excellent physical condition, despite her old age. She had great physical endurance as she notably fully recovered from four <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a> aimed at her by <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> and some <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a>. Although she was hospitalised due to the severity of her injuries, many noted that the four spells straight to the chest could have been fatal, another testament to her overall strength.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Minerva, true to being a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>, had an extremely strong willpower and moral compass. She was able to muster the strength to refuse to marry <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">McGregor</a>, whom she was very much in love with, to avoid having to stop using magic, and after the death of her husband <a href="/wiki/Elphinstone_Urquart" title="Elphinstone Urquart">Elphinstone</a>, Minerva remained dedicated to serving <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a>, her strong will masking the grief and suffering she felt from all except <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>. Indeed, she was held in high regard by the many denizens of Hogwarts during her time as a teacher there, due to how strict, firm and uncompromising she was when dealing with others, which made her one of the most respected (and to some degree feared) <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professors</a> in Hogwarts. When being personally inspected by the high-ranking <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> official <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> during the latter's reign as <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">High Inquisitor</a>, Minerva refused to be intimidated and went so far as to stand up to the latter and mock her in defiance. Even when outnumbered in her confrontations with the Ministry officials who attempted to arrest Dumbledore in the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Office" class="mw-redirect" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Office">latter's office</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> who attempted to evict Hagrid from <a href="/wiki/Hagrid%27s_Hut" title="Hagrid&#39;s Hut">his hut</a>, Minera was quick to intervene on her friends' behalf, only standing down upon Dumbledore's orders on the first occassion and being incapacitated by an egregious attack on the second. During both <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_Wars" title="Wizarding Wars">Wizarding Wars</a>, Minerva remained staunch in opposing <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> even if she did fear speaking his name, which she soon overcame, despite the losses of many of her friends and even when all hope seemed lost with Dumbledore dying and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> taking over, Minerva continued to oppose Voldemort and help protect the students from <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">the Carrows</a>. She defiantly led the defenders during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and even faced Voldemort himself despite <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s apparent death seemingly rendering the Dark Lord unbeatable. Minerva's moral compass also remained steadfast even in the face of great victories as she did not hesitate to take 150 <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">House points</a> from Gryffindor to punish Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville</a> despite how close Gryffindor was to winning the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a> and she remained adamant in confiscating Harry's <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> even though it would greatly benefit the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>.</li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: Being the Head of <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Minerva was an extremely skilled and efficient teacher during her time in this position and was one of the few professors at Hogwarts who could keep a class quiet with minimal effort as a result of her strict nature, making her one of the most respected teachers at Hogwarts. Her effective teaching methods were enough for her to pass <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s inspection of her despite Umbridge's attempts to discredit many Hogwarts teachers along with making her the <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Headmaster" title="Deputy Headmaster">Deputy Headmistress</a> of Hogwarts and later the Headmistress after <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s final defeat.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_wand" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s wand">Wand</a></b>: Minerva's <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a> was 9½ ", <a href="/wiki/Fir" title="Fir">fir</a>, and had a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_heartstring" title="Dragon heartstring">dragon heartstring</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>. The wand was well suited to <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>, proven by its owner, who was a teacher of the subject and an Animagus.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_hornbill" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s hornbill">Hornbill</a></b>: This male hornbill was owned by Professor McGonagall from 1992 or earlier. In that year, she used the <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">bird</a> to demonstrate the spell <i><a href="/wiki/Vera_Verto" title="Vera Verto">Vera Verto</a></i>, in front of her second-years' class.<sup id="cite_ref-COSF_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COSF-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_walking_stick" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s walking stick">Walking stick</a></b>: Minerva used this walking stick after leaving <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, after being hit with four <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a>. It was once borrowed, with her permission, by <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> to chase and whack Dolores Umbridge with.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_office" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s office">Office</a></b>: Minerva's office was a small study located off of the first-floor corridor,<sup id="cite_ref-Corridor_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Corridor-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Floor_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Floor-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> to the right of a <a href="/wiki/Staircase_between_the_first-floor_and_Serpentine_corridors" title="Staircase between the first-floor and Serpentine corridors">staircase</a> to the Serpentine Corridor.<sup id="cite_ref-GF12_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF12-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> It had a large fire,<sup id="cite_ref-Corridor_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Corridor-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> windows overlooking the Training Grounds<sup id="cite_ref-PSF_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSF-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> and the Quidditch pitch,<sup id="cite_ref-Pitch_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pitch-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> and a sparse stone-floored bedroom behind a concealed door.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Office" title="Headmaster&#39;s Office">Headmaster's Office</a></b>: Upon assuming the headship of Hogwarts following the legendary <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Professor McGonagall presided henceforth over the school from the office of her predecessors. It is unknown what, if any changes she did to the decor, or what the passwords were.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Elphinstone_Urquart_and_Minerva_McGonagall%27s_Hogsmeade_cottage" title="Elphinstone Urquart and Minerva McGonagall&#39;s Hogsmeade cottage">Cottage</a></b>: During their marriage in the 1980s, Minerva and <a href="/wiki/Elphinstone_Urquart" title="Elphinstone Urquart">Elphinstone Urquart</a> lived in a small cottage, which the latter purchased after he proposed to her in the summer of 1982. The cottage was located in <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>, from where Minerva could go to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> every day to teach.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorebio_1-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorebio-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall%27s_dress_robes" title="Minerva McGonagall&#39;s dress robes">Dress robes</a></b>: Minerva wore a set of dress robes to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, which was held on <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas Day</a>, 1994, together with a hat on which she arranged a rather ugly wreath of thistles. The robes were made of a red tartan fabric.<sup id="cite_ref-GF23_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF23-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Harp" title="Harp">Self-playing harp</a></b>: Minerva owned an <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">enchanted</a> harp, that could play by itself.<sup id="cite_ref-WUBE_Lost_Love_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WUBE_Lost_Love-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>Professor Dumbledore is a very great wizard, Potter, he has many demands on his time —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>But this is important.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Minerva McGonagall and Harry Potter in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, her dear friend and colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva knew <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> for the majority of her life. She attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as a student during Dumbledore's time as <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> Professor and even replaced him as Head of Transfiguration when he took the position of Headmaster of the school. Albus discovered Minerva in tears in her classroom late one evening after she found out about <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">Dougal McGregor</a>'s marriage with another woman. She confessed the whole story to him, and he offered both comfort and wisdom; telling her some of his own family history, previously unknown to her.
</p><p>The confidences exchanged between the two intensely private and reserved characters were to form the basis of a lasting mutual esteem and friendship. Despite this fact, she had never been fully in his or Dumbledore's confidence. Minerva was one of only a handful of people who knew how dreadful a moment it was for Dumbledore when he made the decision to confront and defeat the Dark wizard <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> in <a href="/wiki/1945" title="1945">1945</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva served for many years as his <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Deputy Headmistress</a>, standing in for him in dangerous situations and even replacing him as Headmistress on several occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> She also served more than once to bring Dumbledore back on track when he became distracted from the matter currently at hand.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Minerva had great faith in Dumbledore, placing great stock in the differences between him and Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> However, she didn't hesitate to disagree with him when she felt the need to do so, greatly opposing his decision to place Harry Potter with <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Dursley</a>'s family<sup id="cite_ref-PSF_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSF-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> and his policy of allowing Harry to run extreme risks.
</p><p>Minerva never hesitated in displaying her loyalty to Dumbledore. When <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> brought Aurors to arrest Dumbledore in 1996, she boldly stepped forward and announced her intention to fight the Aurors on his behalf. She only stepped back at Dumbledore's insistence when he reminded her that Hogwarts and her students would need her in his absence.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Minerva was devastated when Dumbledore was killed in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> during the Battle of the Astronomy Tower and arranged his funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> A year later, when Harry was on a mission given to him by Dumbledore, she didn't question the decision of the late headmaster, but immediately sought to provide whatever assistance she could.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You couldn't find two people who are less like us. And they've got this son — I saw him kicking his mother all the way up the street, screaming for sweets. Harry Potter come and live here?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall discussing the Dursley family as Harry's guardians<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, student, protege, and ally</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva showed her care for Harry ever since she, Dumbledore and Hagrid left him in the care of the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>, in part because she had been quite fond of Harry's late parents. She was sort of a loving grandmother to him and expressed concern with both Dumbledore's choice trusting Hagrid to safely transport Harry to <a href="/wiki/Little_Whinging" title="Little Whinging">Little Whinging</a>, and of the choice of family with whom Harry would stay. She spent hours on end spying on the Dursleys to get an insight to what life for Harry growing up would be like,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> calling them "the worst sort of Muggles imaginable".<sup id="cite_ref-PSF_40-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSF-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>  It is unlikely, however, that she kept watch over Harry, as she would never go against Dumbledore's actions, no matter how much she disagreed with them.
</p><p>When Harry arrived at Hogwarts, Minerva was naturally pleased that he was sorted into Gryffindor, her house and as he studied in Hogwarts. Although her relationship with him remained mostly normal, she kept a watchful eye on him and his friends <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> to ensure his safety. She also (along with the other professors) reported that he was likeable, humble and talented.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Although she was fully willing to punish him for his misdeeds, Minerva would not hesitate to intervene in their affairs whenever necessary to keep them safe and ensured that Harry would not be punished too severely. This was shown when Harry and his friends were caught sneaking around the tower in the dead of night during their first year at Hogwarts and she sent him off to serve detention in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>.
</p><p>
However, rather than punishing or expelling him for having broken Madam Hooch's order that no student would ride on their broomsticks and the risk he took, Minerva brought him to see <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Wood" title="Oliver Wood">Oliver Wood</a>, captain of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>, announcing that she had found their new <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>. In her gratitude for Harry accepting the position, she bought him a <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2000" title="Nimbus 2000">Nimbus 2000</a> for his first Quidditch game.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Her affection for him even allowed her to forgive him and Ron's use of the Weasleys's flying car to reach Hogwarts, which risked exposure of the wizarding world and broke several of the international laws, a far more serious deed than smuggling Norbert out of Hogwarts, without even taking House Points from Gryffindor and only punishing him and Ron by giving them both detention. She nearly smiled when Harry pointed out how she couldn't take House Points for Gryffindor as it was only the beginning of the year.</p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png/revision/latest?cb=20151216143647" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="152" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png" data-image-key="McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20151216143647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png/revision/latest?cb=20151216143647" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20151216143647" decoding="async" width="235" height="152" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png" data-image-key="McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20151216143647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:McGonagallWithHandOnHarrysShoulder.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">McGonagall comforting Harry after refusing to allow him to go to Hogsmeade</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p> This particularly strong concern for Harry, clearly above what Minerva felt for most other individual students, was later shown in his third year: She proved she cared far more for Harry than winning the Quidditch Cup for Gryffindor, ensuring he was kept in maximum security and limiting his time to practise and even not hesitating to confiscate the <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> he was given to out of concern it was sent by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and instantly lost her temper when <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Wood" title="Oliver Wood">Oliver Wood</a> suggested Harry be allowed to fall off his broom as long as he caught the Snitch, intimidating Wood into submission. She also pitied him for being unable to go to <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> due to not having a signed note and appeared to indicate she would be willing to allow him to go had it not been for the danger of Sirius.
</p><p>When Harry became the fourth Triwizard Champion, Minerva adamantly defended Harry from the accusation of <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a> that Harry had been willing to die for the gold rewarded and even went as far as to try to convince Albus into not letting Harry compete, being utterly mortified by the fact that Snape and Dumbledore were willing to use Harry as a bait and often showed herself to be more protective of Harry than the then Headmaster. She also wanted to keep Harry out of the explanation the imposter was about to give, believing Harry had had enough, but reluctantly conceded to Dumbledore's wish that Harry stay. However, she was quick to praise his performance and assure he was tended to in the First Task and helped him train for the Third Task by lending her room.
</p><p>In Harry's fifth year, Minerva promised Harry that she would do whatever she possibly could to see that he achieved his dream of becoming an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>. She supported him unequivocally even though she had never been fully in his confidence. When she later found out about the sort of <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">punishment</a> Harry and various other students had been receiving from <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, Minerva expressed nothing but absolute disgust and disapproval, despite the power Umbridge wielded.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In return, although Harry disliked her strictness regarding his opposition of Umbridge, he was still grateful for her care towards him and was utterly infuriated when McGonagall was attacked so severely by the Aurors sent to capture Hagrid she had to be sent to St Mungo to the point where he even believed Umbridge being murdered brutally (fed to a <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewt</a>) was not a punishment good enough and immediately felt such anger that he coldly defied Umbridge when she gloated over McGonagall's current state despite being cornered.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Why would Harry Potter try to get inside <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw_Tower" title="Ravenclaw Tower">Ravenclaw Tower</a>? Potter belongs in </i>my<i> House!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall's pride that Harry belongs in her house<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Shortly prior to the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Amycus Carrow - who, along with his sister <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a>, had been posted at the school by Voldemort - demanded to know where Harry was in the Tower and McGonagall asked why he would be there as he belonged in her house, with clear pride in her voice. When Amycus spat at McGonagall, Harry was outraged to the point of attacking him with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, even agreeing with <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>'s assertion that one had to "really mean it" to perform the curse correctly. Although shocked by Harry's sudden appearance and his use of an <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curse</a>, she was clearly touched by the gesture. Though Minerva initially tried to convince Harry to flee out of concern for his safety, she immediately joined Harry in retaking the castle and preparing for battle. She did this when he informed her that he was acting on Dumbledore's orders. Nearing the end of the Battle of Hogwarts, Minerva's devastation was great when she saw <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> carrying Harry's seemingly dead body. This grief was enough to make her duel Voldemort head on in the final battle, alongside <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, in order to protect the rest of her students. When the battle ended with Voldemort's death at Harry's hands, she was among the first to embrace him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_8-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>The two continued to have a very positive relationship over the following years. Harry acted as a frequent guest lecturer on Defence Against The Dark Arts, under Minerva's jurisdiction. She would serve as Headmistress over Harry's three children, and in turn she learned to expect them to get into the same kinds of trouble as their father. This was to be expected, after having now taught and served over three generations of Potters. Minerva's relationship with Harry experienced a brief strain when he blackmailed her into using the Marauder's Map to ensure Albus and Scorpius remains apart, which she felt great discontent at doing, but it was reconciled when Harry apologised and she wasn't shown to hold any ill-will afterwards.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger">Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Ah, of course. There is no need to tell me any more, Miss Granger. Which one of you will be dying this year?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall discussing a previous Divination lesson<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521112839" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Granger 2.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140521112839" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521112839" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140521112839" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Granger 2.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140521112839" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, her student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva took a shine to Hermione Granger since the younger witch successfully transfigured a match into a needle early on in her first Transfiguration lesson, before any other student. She gave Hermione one of her "rare smiles". Hence, Minerva was extremely shocked and disappointed in Hermione when she said she had gone looking for the <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">Troll</a> that invaded <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, under the impression that she could stop it. The claim wasn't true, but Minerva was none the wiser.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> When Hermione was attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Basilisk</a> in 1992, Minerva was greatly moved and would often take time to visit her Petrified student in the hospital wing.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_14-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Hermione's third year, Minerva went to the effort to arrange for Hermione to be given permission to use a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to take additional classes. Teachers didn't often seek permission for a student to use one of the devices, but she saw something special in Hermione and went out of her way to make sure the younger witch wasn't under-achieving.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Hermione further showed her high regard of Hermione, by appointing her a Gryffindor <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> in her fifth year at Hogwarts. When Minerva was attacked by several Ministry employees outside of Hagrid's Hut, Hermione showed deep emotion towards the event, like Minerva did a few years before. She and McGonagall were allies during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, surviving the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p><p>Minerva was a role model for Hermione and both had much in common. They both believed that <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> was a very "woolly" subject and that <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a> was a fraud,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, both were considered for Ravenclaw, but in the end were both Sorted into Gryffindor House.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley">Ron Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>That was bloody brilliant!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>Well, thank you for that assessment, Mr Weasley. Perhaps it would be more useful if I were to transfigure Mr Potter or yourself into a pocket watch? That way, one of you might be on time.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; McGonagall's first interaction with Ron<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101104210200" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101104210200" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, her student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron Weasley was a student at the time McGonagall was a professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. He was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>, McGonagall's house. Ron thought she was very strict, however, he did see her good side on a number of occasions. The two clashed when he and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> flew <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>'s flying car to Hogwarts. However, she didn't wish to see them expelled. During the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, Minerva showed the other students how to dance by dancing with Ron in front of the whole class, a move which prompted laughter from the class and Fred and George agreeing to always tease him about it.
</p><p>Ron is appointed <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> by McGonagall in his fifth year after most likely being persuaded by Dumbledore, as he felt that Harry had enough responsibilities to deal with. He and McGonagall were allies during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, surviving the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>It's high time your grandmother learned to be proud of the grandson she's got, rather than the one she thinks she ought to have — particularly after <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">what happened at the Ministry</a>.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall complimenting Neville for the first time<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/67/Neville-longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100601103405" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville-longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville-longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/67/Neville-longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20100601103405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/67/Neville-longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100601103405" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/67/Neville-longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20100601103405" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville-longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville-longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/67/Neville-longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20100601103405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville-longbottom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, her student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva had a long history with the <a href="/wiki/Longbottom_family" title="Longbottom family">Longbottom family</a>, being allies with the Order of the Phoenix, in which Neville's parents were members. They were eventually tortured into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. She also had a personal relationship with Neville's grandmother, who raised him.
</p><p>McGonagall frequently seemed to expect more from Neville than he produced, starting with Neville's first day at Hogwarts when he ran out of a crowd after his toad.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> When Neville "lost" his scrap of parchment (which was actually stolen by <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a>) with Gryffindor's passwords on them, allowing <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> to enter the common room, Minerva was furious with him.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> She voiced pride in Neville's courage in participating in the fight with the Death Eaters in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>. 
</p><p>Minerva couldn't help but feel pity for Neville after the loss of both his parents, whom she knew and fought alongside earlier on in her career. She also sought to encourage Neville to take <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a>, in his sixth year, despite his grandmother's dismissal of the subject as "soft;" Minerva wanted to see Neville pursue his own talents rather than the skills his grandmother appeared to value.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_16-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> After the Second Wizarding War, Minerva may have been the one to employ Neville as the school's new <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> professor.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Draco_Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>What utter rubbish! How dare you tell such lies! Come on — I shall see Professor Snape about you, Malfoy!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall after catching an 11-year-old Draco out of bed<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623202530" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="235" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg" data-image-key="Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140623202530" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623202530" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140623202530" decoding="async" width="165" height="235" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg" data-image-key="Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140623202530" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco-Malfoy-promo-draco-and-slytherin-22383941-1920-2560.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, her student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> favoured students of his own house and often overlooked any misbehaviour from students like Draco Malfoy, McGonagall had little tolerance for nonsense from any student, regardless of their house, and took no notice of the Malfoy family's status within the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding community</a>. As she wasn't a Slytherin, Malfoy didn't respect her at all but was never foolish enough to make this clear in front of her. 
</p><p>Despite her clear disapproval of Malfoy's pure-blood supremacist leanings, McGonagall sought to protect him as much as every other student, being completely appalled when <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> in disguise) <a href="/wiki/Human_to_ferret_spell" title="Human to ferret spell">transformed</a> Draco into a ferret in 1994. She transformed Malfoy back into his human form and reminded Moody that they never use transfiguration as a punishment. In addition, Minerva wouldn't accept Harry's accusations of Malfoy mailing a <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">cursed necklace</a> without sufficient evidence, nor condone any attacks Harry made on Malfoy such as when the former used the <a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a> curse (not knowing exactly what it did) on Malfoy, in 1997.
</p><p>However, when Draco was proven to have led a group of Death Eaters into the castle, Minerva came to see him as much an enemy as any Death Eater, until after the war, where Draco was pardoned. At which point.
