Minerva and Draco established a cordial relationship, as she accepted Draco's <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">son</a> into Hogwarts and treated him just as she would every student despite whatever dark feelings she may had towards Draco for his misdeeds, being utterly appealed at Harry's request that she help Albus and Scorpius stay apart. Draco also trusted her into using the Marauder's Map to find his son and Albus and fully accepted whatever punishment would be given to Scorpius, acknowledging he believed her decision would be fair.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="142" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="245" height="142" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a> get along well, considering they were all in <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a> and fellow members of the Order of the Phoenix. However, Minerva disapproved of <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>'s behaviour at school, although she still seemed impressed by their magical skills. When <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> was appointed as High Inquisitor for Hogwarts, she allied with the twins and attempted to oppose Umbridge.
</p><p>Minerva was fond of all the Weasley children, including <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>. She was glad that Ginny was sorted into Gryffindor, and, although Ginny thought McGonagall was a little strict, she believed that the Transfiguration professor was also fair. Both witches tried to oppose Umbridge (in 1995) and the Carrows (in 1998). Furthermore, Minerva had high regard and expectations of <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>, who was a Gryffindor prefect and <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a> in his last year at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Marauders_and_Lily_Evans">The Marauders and Lily Evans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Marauders and Lily Evans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: The Marauders and Lily Evans"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Is it true, Albus? Lily and James... are dead?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall's devastation regarding the Potter's murders<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/The_Marauders.png/revision/latest?cb=20100821220214" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Marauders.png" data-image-key="The_Marauders.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/The_Marauders.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20100821220214" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/The_Marauders.png/revision/latest?cb=20100821220214" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/The_Marauders.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20100821220214" decoding="async" width="245" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Marauders.png" data-image-key="The_Marauders.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/The_Marauders.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20100821220214" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Marauders.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">The Marauders</a>, her former students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall had long been the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> professor at Hogwarts by the time <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a> attended as students, all being sorted into the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house. After they left Hogwarts, both McGonagall became allies with her former students, who became members of the first Order of the Phoenix.
</p><p>The Marauders were four great friends: <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>. Despite their boisterous ways, at odds with Minerva's no-nonsense reputation, they seemed to have a good relationship with her. Coincidentally, both McGonagall and the Marauders had the accomplishment of becoming Animagi. This information most likely not privy to her.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 176px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="174" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20140712171247" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20140712171247" decoding="async" width="174" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20140712171247" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_Potter1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a>(née <b>Evans</b>), one of McGonagall's best students and an ally in the first Order of the Phoenix</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva liked James Potter (an intelligent and talented wizard), despite the fact that he could sometimes be a bit of a bully and was not above bending the rules. McGonagall seems to have had a good relationship with his future wife, Lily Evans<a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">.</a> The couple would later become <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Girl</a>; neither appointment would have happened if their Head of House had not approved, which means she trusted them. McGonagall was devastated at the murder in 1981 of Lily and James, both of whom she considered her all-time favourites. She later became friendly with the Potters' son, Harry, who was also her student and a member of her House, though she did not show favouritism and was more than willing to take many points even from her own House for misbehaviour.
</p><p>A little over a decade after he left Hogwarts, Remus Lupin (a former <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a> of her House) returned to the school in order to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, becoming Minerva's professional colleaguein 1993. She didn't care about the fact Remus was a werewolf, because Dumbledore trusted him, and respected his efficient teaching skills, as she referenced him during Harry's <a href="/wiki/Careers_Advice" title="Careers Advice">Careers Advice</a>. The two  were members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. After Dumbledore's death, McGonagall, Lupin and several other individuals were devastated; they all discussed about the way Snape killed Dumbledore. Sadly, Lupin himself died in the Battle of Hogwarts.
</p><p>Minerva had a good relationship with Sirius Black. But after James' death, she, the rest of the wizarding community, assumed it was Sirius who betrayed the Potters since he was expected to be their <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a>. Only in 1995 did she learn that the Secret-Keeper at the time of the Potters' deaths was actually Peter Pettigrew, who took the title after Sirius turned it down. Sirius was murdered by his own cousin <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> in 1996. Minerva's reaction to Sirius's death is unreported.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Hero-worshipped Black and Potter. Never quite in their league, talent-wise. I was often rather sharp with him... Stupid boy... Foolish boy...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall's low opinion of Peter Pettigrew<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>Minerva had a pretty poor relationship with Peter Pettigrew, describing him as a "stupid" and "foolish" boy. She confessed that she was harsher than necessary with him during their time together as student and teacher, even when "hero-worshipped" James Potter and Sirius Black for the mischief. Peter faked his own death standing up to Sirius, who was a suspect in the Potters' betrayal, leading McGonagall to regret that she had been harsh towards him and to acknowledge him as a brave Gryffindor.
</p><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rubeus_Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I'm not saying his heart isn't in the right place, but you can't pretend he's not careless.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall's opinion of Hagrid in delicate situations<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" decoding="async" width="165" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, her friend and colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rubeus Hagrid respected McGonagall. Hagrid was the gamekeeper, and later <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> professor of Hogwarts. McGonagall was one of the most serious professors at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and sometimes disapproved of Hagrid's behaviour, especially during the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>. However, they were still close friends, were both members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, and admired Albus Dumbledore.
</p><p>Hagrid once kissed McGonagall on her cheek when he had drunk very much and she was noted giving a flushed giggle in the event's festivities. When Dolores Umbridge and several <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> from the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> sought to sack and exile Hagrid from the school grounds by force, Minerva quickly flew to his aid, in turn taking four stunners simultaneously to the chest. Hagrid was disgusted when the Aurors stunned and injured her to the point that he attacked them in an uncontrollable rage before fleeing, furiously denouncing them as cowards.
</p><p>In 1997, after Albus Dumbledore's death, Minerva stated that she appreciated Hagrid's opinion very much, as did Dumbledore. McGonagall and Hagrid fought against <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. They were among the first ones to run to congratulate Harry after he defeated Voldemort. They both survived the war and still taught at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>And Potter — do try and win, won't you? Or we'll be out of the running for the eighth year in a row, as Professor Snape was kind enough to remind me only last night...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall after enduring taunting from Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="165" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, her colleague and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was Severus Snape's professor of Transfiguration during his time as a student at Hogwarts. After he had graduated and then returned as the <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a> master, he and McGonagall became colleagues. As Head of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>, McGonagall and Snape teased one another about House points and Quidditch standings, acting like friendly rivals to one another. Like Snape, McGonagall was a strict disciplinarian, but was fairer to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, who was a member of her House. 
</p><p>Both were demanding and effective teachers, unusually talented at magic, and loyal to Albus Dumbledore, so over time, Minerva grew to respect Severus despite his dark past. McGonagall knew that Snape was a Death Eater in his youth, but she followed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> in believing that he truly regretted his former allegiance. She did, however, admit to being suspicious of Snape's true allegiance though she trusted him simply because Albus did. Unusually for Snape, he was on first name terms with McGonagall, showing a certain level of personal friendship. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Coward! COWARD!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva's fury towards Snape after duelling him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After Snape killed Dumbledore, McGonagall was shocked and perhaps personally hurt to find her formerly-respected colleague a murderer and apparent traitor. When Snape became Headmaster of Hogwarts, she opposed him and his supposed minions the Carrows, without knowing Snape was secretly helping her protect the students from his fellow <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. At the onset of the Battle of Hogwarts, McGonagall and Snape duelled inconclusively; with <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Professor Flitwick</a>'s later help, and Snape fled the school rather than continue the fight. McGonagall, believing his retreat was motivated by fear, called out "Coward!", an insult he particularly detested. Snape was killed by Voldemort during the battle, but she learnt that Snape had killed Dumbledore in a painful act of loyalty to the Headmaster's own orders too late. Following a private conversation with Harry, Minerva later took the controversial decision to add a portrait of Severus Snape to the gallery of old headmasters and headmistresses in her tower office. There is no report that she objected this, which shows that she likely forgave him and came to admire his marvellous bravery.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pomona_Sprout">Pomona Sprout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Pomona Sprout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Pomona Sprout"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Flitwick</b>: "<i>Nothing we do will be able to keep out You-Know-Who indefinitely.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Sprout</b>: "<i>But we can hold him up.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>Thank you Pomona</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>, and Minerva just before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Professor_Sprout.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100616143554" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="259" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Professor Sprout.jpg" data-image-key="Professor_Sprout.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Professor_Sprout.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100616143554" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Professor_Sprout.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100616143554" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Professor_Sprout.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100616143554" decoding="async" width="220" height="259" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Professor Sprout.jpg" data-image-key="Professor_Sprout.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Professor_Sprout.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100616143554" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Professor_Sprout.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>, her longtime friend and colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The relationship between Professor McGonagall and <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a> dates back to when both attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> The two students maintained an excellent relationship, which was kept well into their adulthood.
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> stood to speak during the <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> <a href="/wiki/Welcoming_Feast" title="Welcoming Feast">Welcoming Feast</a> after her introduction by <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, the two professors were both taken aback at this, and even exchange glances of disapproval.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> on <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Minerva and Pomona had the same views on protecting the Castle against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sybill_Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sybill Trelawney">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Sybill Trelawney"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Sybill Trelawney</b>: "<i>Certainly I knew, Minerva. But one does not parade the fact that one is All-Knowing. I frequently act as though I am not possessed of the Inner Eye, so as not to make others nervous.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>That explains a great deal.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Professor McGonagall's obvious disdain for Divination<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Sybill_Trelawney.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070804193243" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="221" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sybill Trelawney.jpg" data-image-key="Sybill_Trelawney.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Sybill_Trelawney.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20070804193243" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Sybill_Trelawney.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070804193243" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Sybill_Trelawney.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20070804193243" decoding="async" width="165" height="221" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sybill Trelawney.jpg" data-image-key="Sybill_Trelawney.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/Sybill_Trelawney.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20070804193243" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sybill_Trelawney.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>, her colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva and Sybill Trelawney weren't the best of friends, barely maintaining civility between them. Minerva had no use for Sybill's subject, <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, believing that Trelawney was a fraud. The only reason Minerva has never spoken ill of Sybill directly was due to her refusal to insult her colleagues.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her dislike for Trelawney and her teachings, Minerva was still disgusted when <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Umbridge</a> unceremoniously and cruelly sacked Sybill. They would grow to understand one another through their shared hatred of Dolores Umbridge during the woman's tenure as <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor. Minerva was there as a literal shoulder for Sybill to cry on, speaking out against Dolores and told her what she thought after the events.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Filius Flitwick</b>: "<i>I suppose you are aware that nothing we do can indefinitely prevent <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">You-Know-Who</a> to enter the school, right? —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Pomona Sprout</b>: "<i>But we can delay it. —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>McGonagall</b>: "<i>Thank you, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona</a>.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; McGonagall's interaction with other members of staff<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140519154841" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="172" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter Movie Pictures-Professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140519154841" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140519154841" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140519154841" decoding="async" width="241" height="172" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter Movie Pictures-Professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140519154841" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_Movie_Pictures-Professors.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva with some of her colleagues</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall seemed to have a good relationship with most of her co-workers at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Among them was <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>. Their fellow <a href="/wiki/Hatstall" title="Hatstall">Hatstall</a> status was a subject of gentle humour between them, with the two Heads of house being amused to think that they might, but for those crucial moments in their youths, have exchanged positions. Flitwick fought alongside McGonagall in the  the upstart of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest?cb=20100310181520" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="257" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" data-image-key="20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest?cb=20100310181520" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" decoding="async" width="150" height="257" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" data-image-key="20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, her friend and colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall was friendly with <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a>, the nurse. Pomfrey seemed to admire McGonagall's magical abilities and strength. This was shown when McGonagall was hit by four Stunners on the chest, as Maadam Pomfrey said that it would have killed most witches of her age.
</p><p>McGonagall was friendly with <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, the caretaker, although they argued many times. During the Battle of Hogwarts, she shouted at Filch, and called him a blithering idiot. Then she sternly ordered him to call <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a>. It is possible that, after the war, McGonagall and Filch were still co-workers.
</p><p>
Minerva was on amicable terms with <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, her former Potions professor. However, she commented on his seemingly cowardly behaviour when he realised the castle was under attack, noting he should take his students and do so if he wished to leave. She said that the two would duel to kill if he attempted to hinder their efforts against Voldemort from inside the castle, stating that it was time for Slytherin to finally choose their alliances. He was taken aback at this and he fled, but later returned with reinforcements of students' parents and residents of Hogsmeade to help with the battle efforts. Both Minerva and Horace battled together against Voldemort alongside Kingsley Shacklebolt in the Battle of Hogwarts.</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 183px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905192348" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="181" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gilderoy Lockhart COS promo.jpg" data-image-key="Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/181?cb=20160905192348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905192348" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/181?cb=20160905192348" decoding="async" width="181" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gilderoy Lockhart COS promo.jpg" data-image-key="Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/181?cb=20160905192348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gilderoy_Lockhart_COS_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the other hand, Minerva had no liking for <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a> whatsoever, the D.A.D.A professor before Lupin. This was due to him being obnoxious, incompetent and insensitive, annoying her with nonsensical advices while being ignorant and unhelpful around the second opening of the Chamber of Secrets. Even as a student, Lockhart was already a vain, annoying attention-seeking troublemaker, to which she held in contempt. Minerva was positively hateful towards Lockhart when he walked in late and oblivious when everyone else was greatly saddened at <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley's</a> impending doom. She full-heartedly supported Snape sending Lockhart to deal with the monster within in the hopes of scaring her incompetent colleague away. When Lockhart resigned due to his self-induced amnesia, McGonagall was cheerful along with the rest of the staff and students at the news.
</p><p>After Voldemort infiltrated Hogwarts, two new professors took the post of <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a> and <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>: <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> respectively. They were loyal Death Eaters, and befitting their status, they taught Dark Arts rather than Defence Against the Dark Arts, devoted <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a> to explaining how Muggles were filthy animals, and often took delight in punishing students with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>. When Amycus spat on McGonagall's face, Harry Potter got very angry and hit him with the Cruciatus Curse. After the war, McGonagall sent the Carrows to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix_members">Order of the Phoenix members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20140511035621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20140511035621" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20140511035621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>McGonagall had a good relationship with most members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Some of them included <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, whom she appeared to be friendly with Kingsley. They fought Voldemort, along with <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, and all of them survived the war. 
</p><p>Other fellow member was <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, who was appointed as <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">DADA</a> professor in 1994. However, he was captured by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>; Barty Crouch was disguised as Moody and became the professor, as he wanted to send <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to Voldemort. McGonagall was very angry by Crouch's teaching methods and shouted at him. It is possible that she had the same opinion of the real Moody, but Moody might have been friendly with McGonagall afterwards. He was killed by Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 157px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png/revision/latest?cb=20161203031453" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="155" height="207" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort Headshot DHP1.png" data-image-key="Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20161203031453" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png/revision/latest?cb=20161203031453" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20161203031453" decoding="async" width="155" height="207" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort Headshot DHP1.png" data-image-key="Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20161203031453" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_Headshot_DHP1.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, a hated and feared enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Having taught <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> during his time at Hogwarts, Minerva had her suspicions about him and shared them with Dumbledore, who also was cautious about the younger wizard. During the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, Minerva joined the fight against Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, using her skill as an Animagi to spy on the Dark Lord's followers and report her findings to the <a href="/wiki/Auror_Office" title="Auror Office">Auror Office</a>. 
</p><p>During his second rise to power, Minerva joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and stayed in Hogwarts during the tenure of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> as <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> and the Carrows to protect her students. She is one of the few people that isn't afraid of standing against the Carrows, as she did defy them many times during the 1997-1998 school year. In spite of her well-known loyalty to Professor Dumbledore, Voldemort and his followers believed that Minerva was both too gifted to lose, and too sensible not to join them fully once their victory was assured. However, she proved him wrong when she defended the school against his army and, along with <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, bravely duelled Voldemort himself during the second part of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. She watched as Voldemort is defeated by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> once and for all finally ending the War. 
</p><p>Like most in the Wizarding world, Minerva was initially wary of speaking Voldemort's name. Noticeably, however, she became unafraid of saying Voldemort's name sometime during the second wizarding war, as she told <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> to not to be afraid of it because Voldemort would try to kill him anyway (though in the book she still referred to him as He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dolores_Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>He has achieved high marks in all his <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> tests —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>I’m terribly sorry to have to contradict you, Minerva, but as you will see from my note, Harry has been achieving very poor results in his classes with me —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>I should have made my meaning plainer, He has achieved high marks in all Defence Against the Dark Arts tests set by a competent teacher.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Minerva insulting Dolores Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="218" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101127041001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101127041001" decoding="async" width="165" height="218" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101127041001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, her enemy and former colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva disliked Dolores Umbridge right from the beginning when the Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher began to invade Hogwarts with her <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a> position and did everything she could in her power to circumvent Umbridge's authority without risking the loss of her job. She was the colleague whom she had more violently clashed with than any other colleague in her long and varied career. During Umbridge's inspections of McGonagall's class, Minerva tried for the most part to ignore Umbridge. This was difficult due to Umbridge's constant interruptions by means Umbridge's soft, girlish cough of "<i>Hem hem</i>". When forced to acknowledge Umbridge's presence, McGonagall treated her with a cold and harsh demeanour.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite Umbridge having the power to put Minerva on probation or even sack her, Minerva was not afraid to show her disgust and hatred of Umbridge to the woman's face. Despite this, she understood that Umbridge had a lot of power and that she was reporting directly to <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, and so Minerva once warned <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to tread carefully around Umbridge. Even so, Minerva vehemently vouched for Harry during their <a href="/wiki/Careers_Advice" title="Careers Advice">Career Advice</a> session, claiming that she would coach him nightly if she had to in order to realise his dream of becoming an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, after Umbridge's furious protests that Harry would never become one. After Umbridge fired <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> from her post as <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> teacher, Minerva even put aside her mild dislike of Sybill to focus even more on her hatred of Umbridge, indirectly stating that the latter's evaluation is incompetent and will not be taken into consideration.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102185120" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Disloyalty Minerva Dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180102185120" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180102185120" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180102185120" decoding="async" width="240" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Disloyalty Minerva Dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180102185120" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Disloyalty_Minerva_Dolores.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge arguing with Minerva McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even when Dolores took over Hogwarts, replacing <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> as Head of the school, Minerva continued to help undermine Umbridge's reign, preferring to watch her struggle with the chaos that was being caused by the students and <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> (and sometimes even helping with it). When Minerva was attacked and sent to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s" class="mw-redirect" title="St Mungo&#39;s">St Mungo's</a>, Dolores was pleased that she at last had complete control of Hogwarts. After she returned to Hogwarts, Minerva did nothing to curb the students' enthusiasm when Peeves chased Dolores from Hogwarts, only lamenting that she could not watch with them because the poltergeist had taken her walking stick to hit Dolores with as he followed her from the school.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Umbridge returned to the Ministry in a high-ranking position and interrogated Muggle-borns, capturing them and imprisoning them to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. However, after the Second Wizarding War, Umbridge was captured by Aurors and sent to Azkaban herself, for the rest of her life.
</p><p>Despite their hatred for each other, both McGonagall and Umbridge share the same <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">patronus</a>: a cat, although McGonagall's resembled her Animagus form.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Media"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=51" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>The name <i>Minerva</i> means "wise." Minerva is the Roman name of Athena, Greek goddess of wisdom, strategy, war, courage, and justice (among other things), which is a name suitable for Minerva's personality. Also, Minerva was the goddess of wisdom, schools, art and commerce, which could connect to her being one of the heads of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>.</li>
<li><i>McGonagall</i> comes from the Scotsman William Topaz McGonagall, who is considered to be one of the worst poets in the English language, although Rowling stated that this has nothing to do with Minerva, she only liked the surname. The Scottish name McGonagall (or McGonigle, McGonegal) is from the Celtic name Conegal, meaning "the bravest," plus Mc, or "son of."</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=52" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li>Minerva McGonagall is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> actress Dame <a href="/wiki/Maggie_Smith" title="Maggie Smith">Maggie Smith</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>. She also provided McGonagall's voice in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Despite being from Essex, her late mother was from Glasgow, so Smith may had picked up that accent, but is less pronounced.
<ul><li>In 2007, Dame Maggie Smith was diagnosed with breast cancer and struggled through the filming of Half Blood Prince (2008) while undergoing the chemo treatments. In 2009, during the filming of Deathly Hallows: Part 2 she developed shingles (a painful skin rash), but still continued the film despite the pain.</li>
<li>From August 2017 onwards, Maggie Smith is the oldest cast member still living in the series, after the death of <a href="/wiki/Robert_Hardy" title="Robert Hardy">Robert Hardy</a> (born <a href="/wiki/1925" title="1925">1925</a>), who played <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Mcgonagall_pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190510131929" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall pop.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall_pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Mcgonagall_pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510131929" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Mcgonagall_pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190510131929" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Mcgonagall_pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510131929" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall pop.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall_pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Mcgonagall_pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510131929" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall_pop.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minerva as a <a href="/wiki/POP!_Vinyl" title="POP! <ul><li>McGonagall's <a href="/wiki/Tabby_Cat" class="mw-redirect" title="Tabby Cat">Tabby Cat</a> <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> appearance is portrayed in the first instalment by <a href="/wiki/Mrs_P._Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Mrs P. Head">Mrs P. Head</a>.</li>
<li>A younger Minerva McGonagall is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Fiona_Glascott" title="Fiona Glascott">Fiona Glascott</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald">Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald</a></i>.
<ul><li>Previously, on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_Wiki" title="Harry Potter Wiki">Harry Potter Wiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_Lexicon" title="Harry Potter Lexicon">Harry Potter Lexicon</a>, McGonagall's year of birth was calculated to be 1935 from her  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i> biography and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Chapter 15 (<i>The Hogwarts High Inquisitor</i>), which reveals she began Hogwarts in December 1956 after working for the Ministry for two years immediately after graduation. This places her graduation in 1954, her first year in 1947, and her birth in 1935, because of her October birthday, she was almost 12 when starting at Hogwarts. Furthermore, her <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i> piece states that she was a student of Dumbledore when he taught Transfiguration ("under the guidance of her inspirational Transfiguration teacher, Albus Dumbledore. It also states that Dumbledore employed her when he was still Head of the Transfiguration department and that she worked under him when he was Head of the department ("offering her a job in the Transfiguration department, under Head of Department, Albus Dumbledore").
<ul><li>However, in <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald">Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald</a></i>, Albus and Minerva were presented as basically being a contemporary and Dumbledore taught Defence Against the Dark Arts first, meaning he couldn't have taught her Transfiguration. Hence, McGonagall's appearance in <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald">Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald</a></i> greatly upset certain fans and generated debates on the matter. In order to force it to work, she (and Dumbledore) have to switch back and forth implausibly in too short of a timeframe in their career, and it extensively ages <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a> (who had two overlapping school years with McGonagall) too. Theories have included:
<ul><li>McGonagall's comments to <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, where she says she had been working at the school for "thirty-nine years" never specified that she taught those thirty-nine years <i>consecutively</i>, which was the assumption for the calculation to work. This could mean Minerva had been teaching as Head of the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> Department for 39 years and not Hogwarts in general. In this case, it only contradicts Minerva's second statement that she had started as transfiguration professor "after working for the Ministry for two years immediately after graduation."<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_10-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>It is also possible that she took a break in her career at some point in her life like <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> or she was in fact outright lying to Dolores Umbridge about her real length of employment at Hogwarts.</li></ul></li>
<li>There is also the possibility that there was another, older Scottish witch of the same name who also taught at Hogwarts before the birth of the Minerva who appears in the Harry Potter books and films, although it would be unlikely that the two are related as the latter inherited her surname from her Muggle father.<sup id="cite_ref-shortstories_11-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shortstories-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Another possible theory is the idea of <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">time travel</a> as this concept has been explored in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</a></i>, where <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> get stranded in the <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a> timeline but were successfully able to summon their parents back from the <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">present</a> to save them. Similarly, there is a possibility that McGonagall travelled back to the early 1910s to fill in <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s previous (or intended) position in <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>, so Dumbledore could instead teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> thus better preparing his students for the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">war</a> to come. If so, it is likely that Dumbledore was able to summon a professor back from the future (which happened to be McGonagall) to fill in the post by sending a out message to her future self in a <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_blanket" title="Harry Potter&#39;s blanket">similar manner</a> like what was used by Albus Severus to summon <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>. Also, in <i>the Cursed Child</i>, she later expresses her disgust about time turners and their consequences towards Albus Severus and Scorpius due to their reckless use of one and towards <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> due to not destroying that. This may also be attributed to a bad experience she had back in those days when using it.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> stated that she always pictured <a href="/wiki/Maggie_Smith" title="Maggie Smith">Maggie Smith</a>, who portrays her in the films, as Professor McGonagall.</li>
<li>Professor McGonagall has the distinction of being the first magical character introduced in the series, when <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Vernon Dursley</a> sees her reading a map in her Animagus form on the morning after the Potters' deaths. Only the three Dursleys are introduced before her. However in the films, McGonagall is the second magical character introduced as <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> appears before her. She is the second overall character introduced in the film series, as well as the first female character introduced.</li>
<li>In the films, McGonagall appears to be older than she is described in the books. The timeline suggests that the character was forty-six when she and Dumbledore left Harry with the Dursleys, was fifty-five when Harry started Hogwarts, and sixty-two by the Battle of Hogwarts. By contrast, Maggie Smith was already in her late sixties at the time that she first played McGonagall.</li>
<li>In the film adaptations, it seems to be a recurring gag to have Minerva delivering alliterative lines; for instance, in <i>Goblet of Fire</i>, she says "behaving like a babbling, bumbling band of baboons", and in <i>Deathly Hallows: Part 2</i>, she says "particular proclivity for pyrotechnics".</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i> there is a painting of a young Minerva McGonagall on the Gryffindor common room wall. The same painting, although in a different frame, can be seen hung at the Grand Staircase interacting with <a href="/wiki/Cadogan" title="Cadogan">Sir Cadogan</a>.</li>
<li>In the film adaptation of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)"><i>Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</i></a>, she led the respectful wand raising to rid the sky of the dark mark from the late Dumbledore's body.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, after casting <i><a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">Piertotum Locomotor</a></i>, Minerva excitedly says to Molly Weasley, "<i>I've always wanted to use that spell!</i>"</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, she tells <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> not be afraid to say <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s name, because he will try to kill him either way. Also before the Battle of Hogwarts, she duels Snape with what appears to be the <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">Blasting Curse</a>, defeating Amycus and Alecto Carrow before Snape Disapparates.</li>
<li>Minerva is partly inspired by <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>'s inspirational English teacher Lucy Shepherd, who taught her what a good book looks like.</li>
<li>In an early draft of the first book, she was called "Madam McGonagle".</li>
<li>Minerva was the first Animagus introduced in canon.</li>
<li>She was the first female character confirmed to have kept her maiden when she married. Later, it was revealed that Hermione Granger also did.</li>
<li>In an interview after the publication of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> had stated that Hogwarts had a different Head by the time Harry Potter's children arrived in 2017, saying that Minerva was "getting on a bit".<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Her stance was eventually changed, as with the release of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</a></i>, Minerva is shown to still be active as of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>'s time at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-CC41_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC41-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Minerva McGonagall and <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> share the same <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">cat</a>.</li>
<li>McGonagall is a playable character in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)</a></i>.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i>, Professor McGonagall can't enter the Gryffindor Common Room despite the fact she is the head of the house and she was in Gryffindor House while student at Hogwarts.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_5-7" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7</a></i>, she didn't bring the <a href="/wiki/Suit_of_armour" title="Suit of armour">suits of armour</a> to life to help in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_5-7" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7</a></i>, before casting the protective enchantments around the castle, she asked Harry for flowers.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes_and_references">Notes and references</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?veaction=edit&amp;section=54" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Notes and references">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall?action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Notes and references
